Page 6

Yesterday's Financial Conference Held Large Meetings in the Morning and Afternoon; Opinions on the Business Tax Plan Sent to the Executive Yuan for Reference; Measures to Abolish Exorbitant Taxes and Levies Passed; Two Savings Societies Prevented from Recruiting Members; Opium Tax Abolished and Limited Time for Complete Eradication; Fourth General Meeting 9

(Nanjing) The fourth general meeting of the Financial Conference was held at 10:30 AM on the 26th. 134 members were present and 7 were excused. Kong Xiangxi chaired the meeting and reported the receipt of four official documents, including a comparative table of the additional levies on land taxes in various counties submitted by the Shanxi Provincial Department of Finance, and a report on the reduction of additional land taxes submitted by the Shaanxi Provincial Department of Finance. The discussion began immediately, with Zhang Shuyong, the director of the Second Group, reporting on the review process of various business tax proposals. The secretary then read out the review opinions and results.

The whole case was of great importance. Wang Chengying and Yang Mianzhong advocated expanding the business tax rate, opposing the review opinions, because Zhejiang Province was undergoing construction, and the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies must be compensated by business tax. Ma Yinchu said that Zhejiang's construction needed other compensatory measures, and strongly denounced the harm of prize-linked savings by the International Savings Society and the Sino-French Savings Society, saying that the financial authorities should not allow them to continue or should find ways to recover the funds. The International Savings Society has already collected 60 million yuan, and if it continues, it will have a great impact on the national economy. Wang Hantao advocated that the business tax rate should be flexible to suit local conditions, allowing for expansion and contraction, and to protect domestic goods and prevent the intrusion of foreign goods. The case should be referred to another committee for detailed review.

Guan Jiyu said that protecting domestic goods should be approached in other ways. He also said that the business tax in various countries uses the turnover as a standard. This kind of transaction tax is equivalent to China's likin, an important tax levy, which is very harmful to the people and violates the fundamental concept of business tax. The collection of business tax should classify industries and grade taxes, making it very simple, because the purpose of collecting this tax is not to raise the tax rate, but to collect it universally, in order to achieve good results. Chen Changheng said that the tax rate should not be increased, and the review results should be added with the words "It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance submit all the original proposals and review opinions to the Executive Yuan, which will then be transferred to the Legislative Yuan for reference when amending the Business Tax Law." Wei Tingsheng argued that in an economic downturn, he did not agree to increase the tax rate, and that the original review proposal should be passed. Zhang Kailian said that the business tax should be moderately increased to 20 per mille. Wu Jiantao advocated that all cases should be handed over to the Ministry of Finance for detailed consideration and handling based on the actual situation in various places.

The chairman said that the provisions of the business tax rate should be flexible, and that if the provinces have opinions, the Ministry can allow them to handle them within a possible range. Reducing exorbitant taxes and levies requires seeking compensatory methods. At present, agricultural products are not valuable, farmers cannot afford the burden, and everyone is trying to restore the rural areas, so taxes should not be increased. The commercial situation is also the same. As long as businessmen can afford it, it is okay to collect more taxes, but the situation varies from place to place, and the local financial authorities should consult with the Ministry of Finance based on the actual situation. Secondly, China cannot determine expenditures based on income, but should use the principle of determining income based on expenditures, saving where possible.

Then Xu Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance, spoke and responded to Ma Yinchu's points, saying that the Ministry of Finance would never allow prize-linked savings to profit from taxation. The two savings societies, the Sino-French and the International, were permitted during the Beijing era and could be resolved through legislative procedures and administrative methods. At this point in the discussion, members believed that the business tax matter could not be resolved in a short period of time, and expressed their agreement to Chen Changheng's amendment. The Zhejiang representatives were dissatisfied with the review opinions and declared their withdrawal of the original proposal. The chairman said that this was not possible. As a result, the case was amended and passed based on Chen Changheng's proposal. The original text was to submit all the original proposals and review opinions to the Executive Yuan, which would then be transferred to the Legislative Yuan for reference when amending the Business Tax Law. If there are any articles of the Business Tax Law that cannot be met, the Ministry of Finance should submit them to the Executive Yuan, which will then request the Legislative Yuan to amend and promulgate them according to law for implementation.

Then, the original proposal of the Ministry of Industry to organize the business tax of various provinces and cities to conform to the original intention of benefiting merchants and enriching taxes was discussed. Regarding the Shanghai Special Zone road deed stamp duty case, and the case regarding the review of the application of stamp duty on bills of lading for foreign shipping companies, the above three cases were all passed according to the review results. After the Second Group's review report proposals were discussed, Ma Yinchu reported on the review process of various cases by the Third Group. Regarding item A of the fourth part of the Minister's discussion on organizing local finances, the resolution on the division of provincial and municipal local revenue and expenditure was passed according to the review opinion, according to the principles of the first case of this group. Regarding the first two items in the draft regulations for determining local budgets proposed by the Directorate-General of Budget, Accounting and Statistics, and the cases of the Hubei, Anhui, and Shandong Departments of Finance, the resolution was passed according to the review results. The central and local budgets at all levels should be compiled and sent within the legal time limit and strictly implemented. Regarding the internal proposal to determine the procedures for reviewing local administrative expenses, the resolution was passed after modification according to the review results.

Finally, the various cases reviewed by the Fourth Group were discussed. The Hunan Provincial Government requested the Central Government to issue a clear order that the national tax agencies should still entrust the provincial local governments to supervise them in the vicinity in order to rectify the case. Zhang Kailian listed various facts in Hunan Province to oppose the review results. Wei Tingsheng said that the central government will set up accounting sub-offices and other audit agencies in various places, and there is no need for local supervision. As a result, according to the review opinion, the national tax agencies have no subordinate relationship with the provincial local governments, and the proposal in this case is prone to confusion with the administrative system and is difficult to establish. Regarding the proposal to request the central government to allocate funds to develop Guizhou's coal and iron ore resources, the proposal that central and local finances should be internally and externally interconnected to achieve balanced development, the proposal that provincial universities should be changed to national universities or subsidized by the central government to improve them, the request that the government order local officials in various provinces to assist in handling the salt affairs reward and punishment regulations, and the request to reduce the autonomous expenses of various counties and reduce the people's burden, the above cases were all passed according to the review results. Finally, Ma Yinchu and other ten people jointly made a temporary motion regarding the ban on prize-linked savings, requesting to prevent the International and Sino-French Savings Societies from recruiting new members, and requesting the Ministry of Finance to send personnel to supervise the funds of these societies. After Kong Xiangxi appointed other members to review them, they were submitted to the general meeting for discussion and the meeting adjourned at 12:30 noon. The fifth general meeting continued at 2:00 PM to discuss the unfinished proposals. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 26th)

(20) Proposal of Chen Changheng et al. that after reducing local land tax surcharges and abolishing exorbitant taxes and levies, in order to maintain the balance of local budget revenue and expenditure, the central government should coordinate the subsidization of local finances; (29) Unifying the name of the land tax and dividing the land tax into provincial and county taxes; (30) Proposal of the Suiyuan Department of Finance to request the central government to compensate Sui Province for the deficit caused by the abolition of likin and the recent abolition of exorbitant and petty donations and taxes; (31) Proposal of the Qinghai Department of Finance to request the central government to assist Qing Province in consolidating border defense; (32) In the future, the central government should adopt a comprehensive planning and long-term and short-term policy to achieve balanced development in assisting various provinces; (33) New projects in various provinces and cities should be reviewed for local financial resources and implemented separately in order of priority; (34) Proposal of the Qinghai Department of Finance to request the National Government to allocate judicial funds to reduce additional land taxes; (35) Reducing expenditures; (36) Proposal to find ways to restore the Zhangku transportation; (37) Seeking rural financial assistance; (38) Cracking down on private minting of silver and copper coins and private issuance of banknotes to clean up the currency policy; (39) Proposal to increase the import tax on wool products and the import tax on foreign rayon and rayon fabrics separately, and to set up two factories to prevent leakage; (40) Financial disclosure; (41) Clarifying the source of corruption; (42) Improving the financial system; (43) Proposal to set up a farmers' silk cocoon loan office to relieve the rural areas and enrich national tax revenues; (44) Proposal to establish the General Editorial Office of the Financial Encyclopedia of the Republic of China; (45) Request to establish a salt administration reform committee as soon as possible to promote the new salt law to maintain the people's food and enrich tax revenues; (46) Request to actively promote the salt law in stages; (47) Proposal to request the Central Bank to set up a branch in Qinghai as soon as possible to activate finance; (48) Proposal to consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to find ways to recover the privilege of foreign banks to issue banknotes as soon as possible to lay the foundation for a unified currency policy; (49) Proposal to include Gansu tobacco in the tax area of ​​the seven provinces to provide relief; (50) In order to vigorously implement the New Life Movement, the Ministry of Finance should quickly formulate regulations on national compulsory savings and compulsory savings for civil servants and soldiers, and the government should order the Central Bank to set up a trust bureau to cultivate integrity and increase the national economy; (51) Proposal to restore the old system of salt administration agencies and abolish the method of auditors concurrently managing administrative affairs to clarify the system and enhance efficiency; (52) Please issue strict orders to the county magistrates in various provinces to hand over the case, and the basic financial talents of the local government should be trained as soon as possible. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 26th)

Situation of Important Cases Passed 11

(Nanjing) The Financial Conference passed many important cases in the morning and afternoon of the 26th. The causes of the most important cases and the results of the review are recorded as follows:

A. One case of the Executive Yuan's submission on measures for abolishing exorbitant taxes and levies. The review results are as follows: Article 1: The Ministry of Finance shall establish a committee to organize local donations, with the Director of the Taxation Department as a member and concurrently the Director of the Secretariat, and appoint a number of specialized personnel as members, divide into groups to handle affairs, each group with a number of provinces as the scope, and carry out the following matters under the command of the Minister of Finance: A. Investigate the donation and tax situation in various provinces, B. Prepare various organization plans, C. Represent the Minister of Finance to make initial contact and detailed discussion with the financial authorities of various provinces and cities, D. Formulate the types of donations and taxes, tax rates, and collection regulations, E. The types of donations and taxes increased by various provinces and cities, the tax rates, or the change in the collection method, shall be reviewed by this committee before being handled in accordance with the legislative procedures, F. Omitted, G. Omitted, H. Formulate the existence, method, and amount of central subsidies to various provinces and cities. Article 2: Each province and city shall establish a donation and tax supervision committee to supervise the implementation of the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies. Except for the provinces and cities that have established a council, the Ministry of Finance shall select five to seven people from among the fair people who have a reputation in the province and city and submit them to the Executive Yuan for appointment as members of the donation and tax supervision committee to organize it. Article 3: The powers of the donation and tax supervision committee of each province and city are as follows: (1) Investigate the exorbitant taxes and levies and the collection situation within the territory; (2) Study the donation and tax organization methods within the territory; (3) State the donation and tax situation and organization methods of the territory to the provincial and municipal governments and financial departments and bureaus; (4) Directly state the donation and tax situation and organization methods of the territory to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance; (5) Report to the Control Yuan the illegal donations and taxes and the illegal acts of personnel of the tax authorities within the territory. Approved after modification according to the review opinion.

B. One piece of the draft law on the financial revenue and expenditure system and the regulations on organizing local taxes and levies submitted by Wei Tingsheng. One report on the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies submitted by the 12th meeting report of the Rural Reconstruction Association. It was reviewed after being merged.

C. Regarding the business tax case, (another telegram)

D. The review opinion on cracking down on private minting of silver and copper coins and private issuance of banknotes to clean up the currency policy: China's currency system urgently needs to be unified and organized. The Ministry of Finance has long stipulated various organization plans. The claim in this case is based on the regulations of the Ministry of Finance and is very practical and feasible. It should be considered established. It is proposed that the Ministry should notify the provinces based on the original laws and orders to effectively crack down. All mint bureaus in various provinces are ordered to stop minting from today. If there are difficulties in remote provinces, they should also truthfully explain them and the parts should be organized separately. Passed according to the review opinion.

E. Rural financial assistance case. Review opinion: The fundamental way to revitalize the countryside is to provide financial assistance. The claim in this case is very important and the clauses are very comprehensive. It should be considered established. It is proposed that the Ministry of Finance should consult with all relevant ministries and commissions as soon as possible, draft detailed and specific plans, and submit them to the Executive Yuan to order the provinces to effectively implement them to save the countryside. Passed according to the review opinion.

F. Please consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to find ways to recover the privilege of foreign banks to issue banknotes as soon as possible to lay the foundation for a unified currency policy. Review opinion: After investigating, there are many obstacles in China's current financial administration. This is due to the fact that foreign banks do not comply with Chinese laws and issue banknotes, which is only one aspect. Please ask the Ministry of Finance to consult with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to negotiate with various countries to order all foreign banks in China to comply with Chinese laws in order to respect sovereignty and benefit finance. Passed according to the review opinion.

G. (1) Ningxia Department of Finance proposed to exempt the income from exorbitant taxes and levies and similar likin, and the central government should raise funds separately to compensate. (2) Shandong Department of Finance proposed to strictly prohibit counties from arbitrarily collecting donations after the budget is announced to alleviate the people's burden. Review results: After investigating, the measures for abolishing exorbitant taxes and levies and the measures for preparing after abolition have been approved in another case. The Ningxia Department of Finance's proposal to exempt exorbitant taxes and levies and to be compensated separately by the central government has been included in the previous case. Arbitrary allocation is more painful for the people than exorbitant taxes and levies. The Shandong Department of Finance's proposal to strictly prohibit counties from arbitrarily allocating after the budget is announced should be strictly prohibited in accordance with financial principles. Please ask the Ministry of Finance to submit it to the Executive Yuan to notify the provinces to strictly prohibit the arbitrary allocation of counties. Once verified, they will be severely punished to alleviate the people's difficulties. Resolution: Passed according to the review opinion.

H. A. (1) Chen Changheng et al. proposed that after reducing local land tax surcharges and abolishing exorbitant taxes and levies, in order to maintain the balance of local budget revenue and expenditure, the central government should coordinate the subsidy of local finances. Ping-Sui Railway Begins to Organize Debts; East Asia Debts Are Also a Part; Completely Unrelated to Nishihara Loans 15

(Nanjing) The Millers Review said that the Ping-Sui Railway's organization of the Japanese East Asia Xingye Company's loan was the prelude to the Chinese government's organization of the Nishihara loans. According to the person in charge of the Ministry of Railways, the Japanese newspaper reported on May 6 that an agreement to organize the Ping-Sui Railway's 5.2 million yen loan with the Japanese East Asia Xingye Company was signed on April 25. This was true. It was negotiated by the Ping-Sui Railway Bureau and East Asia and approved by the Ministry. In the past two years, the Ministry has actively organized road debts, first to improve creditworthiness and second to determine the pre-determined non-projects of each road. Since its implementation, the creditworthiness of the railway has greatly improved and is well known at home and abroad. The Ping-Sui has gradually gained confidence in business since last year. In order to reduce the burden and be considerate of the creditors, it has long established a method for organizing debts and has signed organization methods with 40 to 50 creditors. East Asia is one of the creditors and requested organization based on the case. The negotiation with the Railway Bureau is within the scope of the pre-scheduled plan. As for the negotiation conditions, both the Railway Bureau and the creditors benefit. The Ping-Sui's organization of East Asia's debts is part of the Ping-Sui's method of organizing debts, and it is also part of the Ministry of Railways' policy of organizing debts. It is purely a railway affair and is completely unrelated to the Nishihara loans. The Millers Report mistakenly believed that Chen Youren listed the Ping-Sui East Asia loan as part of the Nishihara loans in his article published in 1918, and then published a speech based on this wrong record, which is contrary to the facts. There is no Ping-Sui East Asia loan in the Nishihara loans. The Nishihara loans included seven items of loans and advances: (1) Bank of Communications loan, (2) Wired Telegraph loan, (3) Jihui Railway advance, (4) Jihei Forest and Mine loan, (5) Manchuria and Mongolia Four Roads advance, (6) Gao Xu Ji Shun advance, (7) War Participation loan, all of which have their own history. I don't know why Chen Youren mistakenly listed the Ping-Sui Road East Asia loan in it, and Millers misunderstood it. (Special telegram on the 25th)

Statement by Administrative Authorities on the Issue of Traffic and Postal Service. The Japanese Side Has Indeed Proposed a Solution, but Our Government Has Not Yet Discussed It 16

(Nanjing) Regarding the various issues of traffic and postal service, there has been much noise recently, and newspapers in Shanghai and Ping (Beiping) have published conflicting reports and various rumors, making it difficult for the public to know the truth. A reporter from the Central News Agency, considering the importance of this matter, specially visited the administrative authorities at their official residence on the morning of the 26th to inquire about the true situation. According to the authorities, regarding the postal issue, only the Advisory Committee of the League of Nations recently resolved on a method for mail from various countries to pass through Manchuria. This matter is merely a technical method for administrative organs to maintain postal services and is by no means a relationship between governments. However, our country has not yet discussed this matter with Japan, and the reports in various newspapers are not factual. As for the traffic issue, the Japanese side has indeed recently proposed a study to our responsible officials, but it is not a formal negotiation. Moreover, this is only the Japanese side's individual opinion, and our government has not yet discussed it, nor has it made any concrete decisions. The various rumors circulating are all inaccurate. Even if the two sides reach a result through future research, it must first be submitted to the central government for overall consideration before it can be finalized. In short, the central government has always adhered to the principle of not violating and not recognizing the puppet organization on this matter; otherwise, there is absolutely no room for consideration. (Central News Agency dispatch, 26th)

(Nanjing) Regarding the issue of postal service in the Northeast, relevant parties have begun to comply with the resolution of the Sino-Japanese Advisory Committee of the League of Nations: "The exchange of mail between member states of the Universal Postal Union and the Northeast is considered a technical issue, not a relationship between countries, and certainly not recognition of the puppet organization." Based on this principle, ordinary postal relations will be restored at an appropriate time, without any connection to the three words "puppet organization." The Ministry of Communications is conducting careful research based on the League of Nations resolution. (Special dispatch, 26th)

Foreign Minister Barthou Declares France Is Not Isolated; Liaison with Allied Nations is Underway; The Door to Disarmament Is Not Yet Closed; However, French Policy Remains Unchanged 20

(Paris) The Chamber of Deputies held a meeting today to discuss foreign affairs. Many people from the diplomatic community and foreign journalists attended to listen. Foreign Minister Barthou attended and delivered a declaration, which was warmly welcomed throughout the venue. Barthou first referred to Austria as a pillar of peace in Central Europe, and France's policy has always been to maintain its independence. As for Poland, it is a friendly and allied country of France, and his recent trip to Warsaw has brought the Soviet Union and Poland closer. Barthou also said that the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations is a major event. Barthou, as a lover of peace, believes that the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations is of great benefit to peace. Barthou recounted his meeting with Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov in Geneva, saying that he had discussed the Soviet Union's accession to the League of Nations with Litvinov. However, regarding the Soviet Union's request to become a permanent member of the Council of the League of Nations, it seems too early to comment on what attitude France will take. Barthou went on to describe his visits to Czechoslovakia and Poland, saying that the people of both countries warmly received him and the friendship was unforgettable. His trip to Warsaw consolidated the alliance treaty between France and Poland in 1921. He will soon go to Romania and Yugoslavia, and any differences between them can be eliminated through this. He will meet with Turkish Foreign Minister Rüşdü on Saturday. It can be seen that France's policy is to connect the emotions of all parties.

Regarding the issue of disarmament, Barthou said that the policies pursued by previous cabinets are still being followed, that is, disarmament is carried out under conditions of security and in pursuit of equality of armaments. However, France cannot ignore military groups outside the official German army, and as long as Germany's rearmament action does not stop for a day, France will not recognize disarmament for a day. In its reply to Britain on April 17 of this year, France stated that it has always believed that the Disarmament Conference should take disarmament as its final result, and that rearmament contrary to the peace treaty should not be recognized by the Disarmament Conference. However, in any case, the League of Nations and the Disarmament Conference are not closed, and the French government has always supported peace and has always been loyal to the League of Nations.

Regarding the Saar region's vote next year, Barthou said that the freedom of voters must be absolutely respected. During the discussion in Geneva this time, any method that would make Saar residents vulnerable to retaliation after voting was firmly rejected. France has not abandoned the rights it obtained from the treaty regarding the Saar issue, which is deeply gratifying. Barthou said that he had stated to Aloisi, chairman of the Special Committee on the Saar issue, in Geneva that effective safeguards must be taken for the Saar residents' vote. Germany's empty promises to guarantee the freedom of voting are insufficient even if they are a formal declaration. At that time, Aloisi and the Special Committee formulated a method that they considered acceptable, namely, "The French and German governments are willing to recognize all measures that the League of Nations can take to protect the Saar residents." However, the German government was unwilling to accept this method, which is regrettable.

Barthou concluded by saying that no one in the French people likes to fight. The French are doing their best to avoid war, and he believes that war can be avoided. The French will always be consistent with their friendly and allied countries. It is not impossible for France and Italy to reach a friendly compromise, and its relationship with Britain has not cooled. At this time, someone raised questions about France's international relations. Barthou replied that France is not in an isolated position. At this point, almost all the members of the venue applauded, including the Socialist Party. The Chamber of Deputies then decided to postpone the question on foreign affairs until the Foreign Minister returns from Geneva, as the Foreign Minister must go to Geneva in the near future, and then adjourned the meeting. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Preparing to Open the Disarmament Conference; Foreign Ministers of Various Countries Go Together 22

(Geneva) Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, arrived here this morning. While talking to people in the Disarmament Conference lounge today, Henderson declared that he does not intend to make any new proposals at this session of the conference. In his opinion, only the countries attending the Disarmament Conference, especially those most concerned with the disarmament issue, can clearly state their intentions at this session and make new proposals when necessary. It is rumored that Henderson supports returning the entire file of the disarmament issue to the Council of the League of Nations as an end. Regarding this rumor, Henderson again denied it today. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(London) Although Britain and France are only separated by a strip of water, their concepts of security are very different. Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, after returning to England from Paris, recently spoke to a special correspondent of a newspaper about two different opinions on the Disarmament Conference. First, in Henderson's view, the best way to get Germany back to Geneva is to have the entire General Committee of the Disarmament Conference reiterate the declaration of December 11, 1932, in which the five major powers allowed Germany to obtain the right to equality of armaments within the scope of security. Second, Henderson is most opposed to transferring the negotiations on the disarmament issue to the Council of the League of Nations. He said, "I don't see any benefit in such a method. It is undoubtedly impossible for Germany to attend the Council of the League of Nations. As far as the interests of small countries are concerned, their representatives on the Main Committee on Disarmament are more numerous than those on the Council of the League of Nations. As for the major powers, their opinions are divided, and therefore all progress has been hindered so far. In the future, it is difficult to expect them to be more harmonious and courageous on the Council of the League of Nations than in normal disarmament negotiations. Moreover, in case of failure, public opinion will blame the League of Nations itself, rather than the politicians representing the countries." According to the five-power declaration of December 11, 1932, the principle to be followed by the Disarmament Conference is to give Germany and other countries that have been reduced in armaments by treaty, in principle, the right to equality of armaments within a security system suitable for all countries. Germany then returned to the Disarmament Conference. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(Paris) The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference will meet in Geneva on the 29th of this month. The United States will still send Davis to attend as an observer. Davis arrived here in the industry today from the United States. Also, Henderson, Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, arrived here from London. Henderson and Davis went to Geneva together in the same car tonight. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) British Foreign Secretary Simon is scheduled to arrive in London on Sunday, and will probably travel to Geneva with Foreign Minister Barthou in the same car to attend the General Committee of the Disarmament Conference meeting on Tuesday of next week. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Poland Has Priority in This Regard 25

Although Paraguay has repeatedly negotiated diplomatically, hoping that Bolivia would abandon this barbaric means, it has been ineffective. Therefore, Paraguay's decision is indeed legitimate. The Paraguayan government, although unwilling to use this barbaric method, has no choice but to use the same method to treat Bolivia. (Havas dispatch, 26th)

(Geneva) The Secretariat of the League of Nations announced today that France, Ireland, Sweden, and Lithuania have also notified that they accept the proposal to embargo arms to Bolivia and Paraguay. (National dispatch, 25th)

Bulgaria Becomes a Hotbed for Global Narcotics Manufacturing: Inflow of Raw Materials Has Increased Greatly in Recent Years, with a Large-Scale Transportation Organization; U.S. Representative Addresses League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee 29

(Geneva) Today, U.S. Representative Fuller, at a meeting of the Opium Advisory Committee, revealed the inside story of Bulgaria's opium and narcotics trafficking. Fuller cited the words of Cairo Police Chief Russell, stating that Bulgaria remains a major source of narcotics manufacturing in Europe, thus attracting villains from all over the world. In 1930, Bulgaria imported only a small amount of materials for manufacturing narcotics. However, by 1933, the amount imported was sufficient to manufacture twelve times the amount of narcotics needed for legitimate purposes worldwide. Bulgaria currently has the world's most well-organized smuggling organization, and a former Sofia police chief is the owner of a narcotics factory, while another Minister of Health is also involved in this business. (Reuters, 25th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Opium Advisory Committee met today, chaired by Austrian Representative Souersitz. U.S. Representative Fuller reported on various narcotics figures to prove that the amount of anhydrous acetic acid manufactured in France and Germany and imported into Bulgaria has greatly increased. This anhydrous acetic acid can be used to manufacture as much as 6,000 kilograms of heroin, while the legitimate global need for heroin is only 1,500 kilograms. Canadian Representative Sherman reported that Bulgaria's opium production was 4,000 kilograms in 1931, increased to 45,000 kilograms in 1932, and further increased by 20,000 kilograms to 65,000 kilograms in 1933. Egyptian Representative Russell explained that in the Macedonian region of Bulgaria, farmers are switching to growing poppies because they cannot sell the tobacco and wheat they grow. Neighboring countries, seeing the profit, may also follow suit, and thus Macedonia has become a hotbed of drug addiction in Europe and the world. Italian Representative Cavasani expressed the hope that the Bulgarian government would take strict measures. The Bulgarian representative then spoke, saying that since the establishment of the new Bulgarian government, his duties in this matter have been revoked. However, the new government is determined to strictly fulfill its obligations, and the measures required by the Advisory Committee will also be taken. This he can guarantee. U.S. Representative Fuller then spoke again, requesting that France, Germany, and Bulgaria submit reports on the export and import of anhydrous acetic acid. The committee subsequently passed a draft resolution stating that Article 15 of the International Convention (established on July 13, 1931, and named the International Convention for Limiting the Manufacture and Regulating the Distribution of Narcotics) stipulates the establishment of a special administrative agency to handle narcotics issues. Governments of all countries should submit reports to the Advisory Committee on the measures taken to establish this agency and the methods to prevent the illegal sale of narcotics. The governments of all countries should also collect information on the anti-drug efforts of various international and domestic narcotics prevention organizations and missionary agencies and report to the committee. (Havas, 25th)

(Geneva) After the Opium Advisory Committee released shocking news yesterday regarding Bulgaria's illegal manufacture and sale of opium and narcotics, the Bulgarian representative declared today that the new government has dismissed the public health official mentioned by Egyptian Police Chief Russell. The new government has requested the League of Nations to provide information at any time so that it can quickly and seriously deal with the sale of drugs. (Reuters, 26th)

Labor Strife in the United States Rises and Falls: Truck Drivers' Strike Ends Peacefully, Situation in the Electrical Industry Remains Serious 30

Minneapolis, The truck drivers' strike that lasted for many days in this city has now ended with the signing of an agreement between the union and employers. The agreement stipulates the rights that workers should enjoy for their years of service, prohibits discriminatory treatment of workers who join the union, and establishes a basis for arbitration to resolve disputes. It also includes clauses regarding wages and working hours. It is generally believed that this result is a victory for the workers. It is estimated that one person died and over a hundred were injured in this labor dispute. (Havas, 26th)

Turkey Orders Restrictions on Foreign Nationals' Employment: From Government Employees to Chauffeurs, All to Be Dismissed and Replaced by Turks 31

Istanbul Today, the government passed an order that foreign nationals employed in certain professions will be replaced by Turks. This order will affect thousands of foreign nationals residing in Turkey. From May 21st to June 21st, all foreign chauffeurs, barbers, tailors, shoemakers, hat makers, translators, guides, stock exchange staff, and musicians must be dismissed. From June 21st to September 21st, all foreign manual laborers must cease operations. From September 21st to November 21st, foreign nationals employed in restaurants, cafes, etc., or street vendors must be dismissed. From November 21st to January 21st, 1935, foreign-owned photography studios and printing houses must cease operations. From January 21st to March 21st, 1935, foreign nationals selling state monopoly goods, performers, singers, and shipping merchants must cease operations. From March 21st to May 21st, all business managers, government employees, and foreign staff in the Turkish government must be dismissed. This order was originally scheduled to be implemented last year, but was delayed due to protests from various governments. The foreign nationals most affected are Greeks, Italians, Persians, and Americans, who have resided here for decades, so their livelihoods will be difficult to resolve. Some foreign nationals may change their citizenship to Turkish, otherwise they may be expelled from the country. The Turkish government claims that there are many unemployed Turks, so it has no choice but to implement this measure. (Reuters, 25th)

(New York) The People's Forum reports that some quarters believe that Britain and the United States are about to hold talks on naval issues, with the intention of forming a common front to deal with Japan's demands to increase its navy, while also forming a British-American agreement to limit Japan's influence in Asia. If the results deem it appropriate to build these cruisers, the U.S. government can then resume construction. The U.S. government did not heed this advice, and Congress has also approved government funding to build another three 10,000-ton cruisers, indicating that there are differences of opinion between the two sides. In addition, British strategy seems to be based on a new principle: that in the event of war, Britain's maritime communication with India should pass through the Cape of Good Hope, rather than through the Suez Canal. The British government believes that the eastern Mediterranean is vulnerable to air strikes, hence this new principle. Relevant Authorities to Strictly Enforce Regulations and Pay Attention to Fishing Industry Registration Applications 68

(Nanjing) Representatives of the aquatic products industry, including Chen Tongbai, telegraphed, stating, "Unscrupulous merchants are organizing fishing companies in Shanghai and plan to purchase fishing vessels from Japan. Please prohibit the issuance of licenses." The Ministry of Industry believes that hand-operated net fishing and motorized trawler fishing are among the licensed fishing industries. While the representatives' presentation is not without merit, considering that the new-style fishing industry still needs promotion and it will not significantly affect ordinary fishing vessels along the coast, it is not appropriate to suspend the issuance of licenses. However, in order to maintain fishing industry laws and regulations and prevent unscrupulous merchants from colluding with foreigners under assumed names, special regulations have been formulated regarding the registration procedures for licensed fishing industries that must be followed. The Executive Yuan has instructed the provincial and municipal fishery administrative departments along the coast to carefully review all registration applications in accordance with these regulations. (Special dispatch of the 26th)

▲London Gold Price: The London gold price today is 136 shillings and 6 pence, a decrease of half a pence from yesterday.

▲London Silver: The London silver market saw buying from the United States and selling from India this morning, with limited trading. The spot price is 19 and a half pence, and the futures price is 19 and 5/825 pence, both down 0.0625 from yesterday.

▲New York Silver: The New York silver market opened quietly, with mixed sentiment. The authorities are insisting on the tax provision in the silver legislation, so speculators have little interest in the silver market. The price is similar to London, with the forward opening price down 10 to 16 pounds from yesterday's closing price.

▲Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market closed quietly today, with both spot and futures prices down. The spot price is 53 rupees and 11 annas.

▲Special Telegram: He Sheng & Co. received a telegram from London on the 26th stating that the London Financial Times' New York dispatch claims that the United States House of Representatives committee has heard opinions from all parties regarding the silver legislation. Treasury experts believe that the London silver market has great influence and can dominate the silver price. If this bill is passed, the world silver price will exceed 50 US cents per ounce. Japanese Puppet Opium Policy - Establishes Daman Company - Capital of One Million Yuan - Poisoning the People of Four Provinces 105

Changchun Dispatch: It is an undeniable fact that Japan wants to use opium to destroy our race. According to investigations, among the 30 million compatriots in the Northeast, as many as 9 million are addicted to opium. They still consider this insufficient. Recently, in view of the opium purchases in Rehe Province and the Xingan West Branch Province, although they are carried out by the buyers designated by the various branches of the Rehe Opium Monopoly Bureau, the current purchase situation in various places has become a trend of individual competition because the buyers' organizations are scattered and lack centralized control. As a result, it is quite difficult to proceed with purchases and there is no way to start, and it has resulted in smuggling. The Japanese puppet authorities have now decided to adopt the organization of the Pseudo-Capital Monopoly Bureau as a countermeasure to this matter. Under the guidance of Takeuchi, the Japanese director of the Chengde Opium Monopoly Bureau, local opium merchants will be united to form the Daman Company, which specializes in purchasing opium produced within the jurisdiction of the Rehe Monopoly Bureau, ensuring that all opium produced goes into the Monopoly Bureau. The general manager of the company is the traitor Zhang Yuxuan, the deputy manager is the traitor Hu Mojie. In addition, all powerful opium merchants in Chengde, Pingquan, Baliwei, Lingyuan, Chaoyang, Chifeng, Weichang, and other places are members of the association. The purchasing agents contribute funds to collect a capital of 1 million yuan in pseudo-currency, and the company was established on April 1st. On April 20th, it received the permission order from the Pseudo-Ministry of Finance. The company plans to purchase 10 million yuan worth of opium in Rehe Province and the Xingan West Branch Province. The Monopoly Bureau charges a handling fee of about one dime per tael for the opium. Since its establishment, it has purchased about 300,000 taels of opium. The company's activities and the locations of the branch offices are listed in detail below: (1) Locations of branch offices and capital allocation: Chengde 40,000, Pingquan 200,000, Lingyuan 70,000, Chaoyang 200,000, Chifeng 300,000, Weichang 200,000. (2) Sub-branches: 5 in the Chengde jurisdiction, 2 in the Pingquan jurisdiction, 4 in the Chifeng jurisdiction, 1 in the Weichang jurisdiction, 3 in the Lingyuan jurisdiction, 5 in the Chaoyang jurisdiction, and branches are also planned to be opened in Fengning, Anjiangtun, and Tiantuzhen. (3) Anti-smuggling measures: 15 secret investigation teams are currently dispatched to the customs and provincial borders and are currently conducting investigations.

Details of the Martyrdom of the Rehe Righteous Army in the Anti-Japanese War - Righteous Army Liu Liangshan Kills 400 Japanese Soldiers - Exhausted Ammunition and No Reinforcements, Surrounded by the Enemy, He Commits Suicide 106

The Wujiazi, Sanjiazi, Weijiagou area, the largest base of the Rehe Righteous Army for the past two years, has been subjected to sieges, burnings, and killings by the Japanese army. According to people from Rehe who recently spoke about the details, Liu Cunqi, commander of the 9th Division of the Rehe National Salvation Army, alias Liangshan, was the bravest of the Rehe righteous army. Previously, he fought with thousands of Japanese troops in Wujiazi and Weijiagou. More than a thousand righteous soldiers and civilians died in this battle. At that time, Liu, wielding two guns, broke through the encirclement and fled into the Dongshan mine tunnel in Weijiagou. Because there were many tunnels, the Japanese army assigned two soldiers to guard each tunnel and withdrew after ten days. Afterwards, the people entered the tunnel and found that Liu had committed suicide. Only one bullet remained in the pistol he was carrying. Those who saw this could not help but weep. Since the Eastern Incident, many patriots in the Northeast have risen up to resist Japan. Few can lead by example and not fear sacrifice like Mr. Liu. As for running out of ammunition and being trapped by the enemy, he still ended his life by suicide to show his steadfast will. It can be said that he was benevolent and righteous to the extreme. No wonder those who saw it wept bitterly. Mr. Liu was originally a sheep butcher. He joined the army in his twenties. Everyone in the Liaoxi area knew Liangshan. Liu had a bald head, so he called himself Liangshan. In mid-January of the previous year, he led patriotic youths from the Northeast to organize the righteous army and recovered Jinxi County. Within more than 20 days, he killed 300 to 400 Japanese soldiers. Japanese newspapers reported that the Battle of Jinxi was one of the battles in which the Japanese army suffered the most casualties after the Battle of Jiangqiao by Ma Zhanshan. The Liaoxi Righteous Army always claimed to be part of Liu's unit. The Japanese army was shocked by his courage and dared not advance. Mr. Liu initially served as the commander of the 36th Route of the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, and later served as the commander of the 9th Division of the Northeast National Salvation Army. The army attacked Yi on October 20th of the previous year and attacked Jin on the 25th. Liu was responsible for the main force in both. He accumulated more than 100 mu of land, had an old wife, and an eldest son about 22 years old, who was married and had a grandson. He also had a second son over ten years old. Now they are all drifting about in unknown places. (Northeast News Agency)

The Fourth Army's Work After Stationing in Longgang: Officers Supervise Road Construction, Soldiers Farm for the People 107

Nanchang Correspondence: Since the fifth campaign against the communists began, the speed of the Northern Route Army's advance has truly set a new record in communist suppression. After the Sixth Route Army captured Shanggu and Longgang, they immediately began building blockhouses and roads. The 59th and 90th Divisions of the Fourth Army made the most effort. The officers of the army went out every day to supervise the work. Although the materials used were locally sourced, they did not harm the people in the slightest. The roadbed was solid, the road surface smooth, and trees were planted along the edges in an orderly manner. The pavilions and public restrooms were also built in the most rational way, making it a model highway in Jiangxi. Furthermore, in the Shanggu and Quejiaping areas, many villages and houses were burned down by the Red bandits, and the residents were also forced to move elsewhere, unable to return, which delayed spring plowing. The 90th Division, after stationing there, used local bamboo, wood, and thatch to build barracks, creating a camp that stretched for ten miles. At night, the lights shone brightly, resembling a city night scene, showing no signs of desolation. The officers and soldiers of the division rested there, climbing mountains and peaks several times a day, training diligently, and showing great spirit, fully demonstrating the vigor of modern soldiers. The nearby fields, because many people had not returned, were about to become barren. Division Commander Ou Zhen and Chief of Staff Huang Zhanchun, believing that spring plowing could not be abandoned, specifically ordered their subordinates to farm for the people, personally leading officers and soldiers to the fields to plant rice seedlings, setting an example for all units. High-ranking officials, after riding horses and reprimanding, then tilling the land themselves, their interest ran high. They plowed and harrowed, looking just like old farmers. The officers and soldiers were happy and harmonious, working hard to cultivate the land. In two days, they planted dozens of acres of fields. The people were all grateful and spread the word, happily coming back one after another. It is heard that orders were also given to officers and soldiers of each regiment to allocate labor to farm for the people, so that the residents could return and harvest. Upon investigation, the bandit areas have been ravaged by the bandits for many years, and now they are seeing the light of day again. The Fourth Army has always been known for its bravery in battle and strict discipline. Now it can also get close to the people, who deeply love and support it. The people's hearts and minds are enough to affect the success or failure of the suppression campaign. Seeing this, it is anticipated that the pacification of the Red bandits will not be far off.

The Anhui Construction Bureau Seeks to Rescue the Rural Economy by Organizing a Design Committee 108

Anqing Correspondence: In recent years, Anhui Province has been plagued by floods and bandit disasters, leading to sluggish sales of agricultural products and a decline in the rural economy, as well as the near collapse of the urban economy. In order to urgently seek relief, the Construction Bureau has specially organized an emergency rural relief design committee. Its design scope includes: (1) Promoting the planting and expansion of improved agricultural products; (2) Promoting the manufacturing and improvement of agricultural products; (3) Removing obstacles to the transportation and sale of agricultural products; (4) Planning for the convenience of the transportation and sale of agricultural products; (5) Controlling and managing special agricultural products; (6) Liaising and communicating with the sales areas of agricultural products in this province; (7) Promoting rural cooperation and regulating rural finance. The bureau has already dispatched Secretary Chen Yan, Wang Shoujiong, Xia Gengying, Section Chief Yuan Fen, Technical Expert Fang Junqiang, Technicians Duan Tianjue, and Hong Changyi as members of the committee, and designated Chen Yan, Yuan Fen, and Fang Junqiang as standing committee members. Preparations are actively underway and it will be established soon (24th).

Dredging Project of the Jiangbei Six Tang Rivers Expected to be Completed by the End of This Month 109

Zhenjiang News: The Jiangbei Six Tang Rivers are crucial for transportation, irrigation, and drinking water for Huaiyin, Suqian, Siyang, Shuyang, Lianshui, Donghai, and Guanyun counties. Since construction began on January 1 of this year, the project has progressed extremely rapidly. The project within the boundaries of Huaiyin and Siyang counties has been completed, and the remaining counties are expected to be completed in the near future. The progress of the river construction and its recent situation are roughly as follows:

This dredging project of the Six Tang Rivers is being carried out entirely in accordance with the three principles determined at the Jiangsu Province Six Tang Rivers Dredging Conference last year: (1) Deepening the riverbed from Xiji to Longgou to ensure smooth discharge; (2) Widening the dikes and canals from Guji to Longgou to increase capacity; (3) Repairing all dikes to prevent flooding. It is estimated that 2 million cubic meters of earth will be dredged and 3.5 million cubic meters of earth will be used for dike repairs. The amount of earthwork, food, and number of workers recruited by each county were also determined by the conference. The lowest price for dike construction was 4 cents per cubic meter, the highest was 6 cents, averaging 5 cents, which was temporarily decided by the engineering office based on local conditions and distance. The excavation of river earth cost 7 cents per cubic meter of mud, and 1 dime per cubic meter of sand and gravel, averaging 8.5 cents per cubic meter, totaling more than 600,000 yuan in labor costs. The number of workers recruited was estimated at 8,000 in Suqian, 6,000 in Siyang, 4,000 in Huaiyin, 14,000 in Shuyang, 10,000 in Lianshui, 6,000 in Donghai, and 12,000 in Guanyun. After the conference closed on November 30, the provincial government immediately appointed Xu Dingkang, director of the Jiangbei Canal Engineering Bureau, as the director of the Six Tang Rivers Dredging Project. Xu departed from Yangzhou for Qing on December 9 and established the engineering office on the 10th, dividing the entire river project into five sections, with one engineer assigned to each section. After that, the river channel was surveyed, and the survey was completed by the end of the year. Dredging began on January 1 of this year, but due to the Lunar New Year, work could not proceed quickly. Later, the engineering office repeatedly ordered the counties to work hard, and the project began to proceed actively. The project within the boundaries of Huaiyin was completed on April 10, Siyang was completed on April 20, and the rest are also 70% or 80% complete. It is expected that the project will be fully completed by the end of May (26th).

Suzhou: The Religious and Philosophical Research Society Promotes Superstition 110

Inside the North Temple on Pingmen Road, a so-called Religious and Philosophical Research Society has recently been established, causing a sensation in society and a frenzy throughout the city. The detailed situation and analysis of its content are as follows:

The society has a Founder's Hall, with an image of a certain Xiao in the center, neither Confucian nor Buddhist, with his hair tied up and holding a clean bottle. In front of the image is a table with an incense burner burning sandalwood, and in front of the table are more than twenty futons. In addition, there is another Light Hall, with a yellow cloth like a screen in the center, and an offering table in front with incense, flowers, and fresh fruit offerings. Two rows of futons are also arranged in front of the table. All who enter to worship must take off their hats and shoes, and enter silently, performing the three kneelings and nine kowtows. Moreover, it is not for ordinary people to enter. Only those who have a certain reputation in society and are considered to have innate good roots can be guided in by people from the society. It is said that after performing the ceremony, gazing at the screen will allow one to see the images of various gods and bodhisattvas as one wishes, but in the end, it is just a kind of rumor. Those from all walks of life who join, regardless of gender, can do so with a member's introduction, and by paying the fee as usual. The procedure is to first worship the image of the founder, kneeling on the futon for about two hours, called "receiving light," and then enter the Light Hall to worship as usual. In this way, one already has the supernatural power to heal people. The society claims to mix Confucianism, Buddhism, and Taoism, and worships the founder Xiao and establishes a separate sect. It takes not feeling a pulse and not using medicine to heal people as its work. After joining the society, one must sacrifice everything and dedicate oneself to the society, even women. The reason is that so-called "adult gentlemen" also join to call on others, so many believe in it. Among the gods worshiped by the people in the society, some never get to see the teacher Xiao in their lives. The other day, he suddenly arrived and gave a public lecture and hosted a vegetarian meal. However, the way Xiao spoke of healing was by silently reciting the positive energy of the twenty characters of loyalty, forgiveness, integrity, and virtue, which is different from the "Bodhisattva save you" that his disciples proclaimed. According to the general public, Xiao is similar to the so-called "senior brother" in the previous Boxer Rebellion. Since the establishment of the society, in less than twenty days, the number of patients from far and near who came to seek treatment has been no less than several thousand per day. Currently, party members Jiang Yuqi and Zhu Mengmei have submitted a report to the county party headquarters, stating that the society has not yet been ordered by the party headquarters to be allowed to prepare, yet it has already claimed to heal people without using medicine or feeling a pulse, causing foolish men and women to flock to it, with no less than one or two thousand people going to seek treatment every day. The method of healing is to have a square of gauze, with the practitioner writing talismans on it, burning it into ashes, and having the patient take it, saying that it can cure the disease. However, those who have been treated have not seen any efficacy, and it is even said that there is a danger of worsening the condition. Such open promotion of superstition, confusing the foolish people, disrupting social perception, and harming the lives of the people, should be reported to the county government, ordering the Public Security Bureau to quickly disband it. According to the report, County Party Committee Standing Member Zhu has sent a letter to the county government to investigate and deal with the matter.

A Boat from Xuzhuang Robbed En Route 111

A boat traveling between Suzhou and Xuzhuang, owned by Ge Huangyao, was passing near Shangfang Mountain in Shihu on the afternoon of the 25th when it was suddenly encountered by a bandit boat with four bandits who, armed with guns, boarded the boat and robbed the passengers. All six passengers were searched, and more than 100 yuan were stolen. Afterwards, the boat owner reported the robbery to the Public Security Bureau to pursue the stolen goods.

Wuxi: Implementation of Cocoon Business Control Leads to Firm Disputes Between Officials and Merchants 112

Since the Construction Department issued the regulations for the control of the cocoon business, the cocoon businesses in this county have had many objections. Therefore, at 2:00 PM on the 24th, an emergency meeting was held at the Silk Factory Association to discuss and decide on four measures to submit to the authorities for a petition to postpone the implementation. The situation was recorded in this newspaper, stating that all requests for funds from unregistered cocoon businesses should be rejected, etc. The disputes between officials and merchants were quite firm. Yan Shenyu, the county magistrate of this county, and Cai Jingde, the deputy director of the model district, considering that the cocoon market was approaching and could not be delayed, went to the province the other day to ask Director Shen of the Construction Department for instructions on how to resolve the matter. After receiving the report, Director Shen was quite firm, stating that the control of the cocoon business is one of the provincial measures to rescue the entire silk industry. The Chinese silk industry has reached its most dangerous point. If improvements are not urgently sought, it will inevitably suffer from international competition and fall into bankruptcy. The livelihoods of farmers and the status of merchants will be fundamentally affected. In any case, there can be no changes. As for the collection of improvement fees, Zhejiang Province has already implemented it last autumn and is collecting it slightly again this year, so there is a precedent. Moreover, the improvement fee is specifically used for improving the silk industry and is different from donations and taxes. If there are a few individuals who do not understand the situation and disregard the future interests of farmers, deliberately obstructing the progress of the project, they will be severely punished. Regarding those who do not follow the procedures for registration and start operating, their cocoon licenses will be revoked. If anyone collects cocoons without registering and paying the deposit, once discovered, the dried cocoons will be confiscated, and a double improvement fee will be collected as a punishment. After receiving the instructions, Yan and Cai returned to Wuxi yesterday morning (26th) and decided to follow the instructions given by Director Shen. Therefore, it is feared that it will not be resolved for a while.

Rice and Bean Industry Changes to New Measuring Instruments 113

The case of promoting the new system of weights and measures in this county has been implemented by most industries one after another. Only the rice and bean industry has been slow to implement it. After repeated urging by the authorities, the Rice and Bean Industry Association has successively sent the measuring instruments used for county inspection. More than 340 pieces have already been inspected and qualified by the county government, and they can be unified.

A Major Silk and Iron Merchant Goes Bankrupt with Millions in Losses 114

Zhou Zhaofu, a resident of Dongfeng in Zhouxin Town, is a major figure in the silk and iron industry, with assets of four to five million. His business operations cover various ports such as Shanghai, Hankou, Suzhou, Wuxi, and Dalian. His father, Shunqing, was a fourth-rank Beijing official in the late Qing Dynasty and even co-founded the Xincheng Bank with Prince Qing Yikuang, causing a sensation for a time. After Shunqing's death, Zhaofu carried on his father's aspirations and continued the business he had created. In addition to the three silk factories in Wuxi, Yuchang, Shenchang, and Dingchang, he also has Xinyuanlai Smelting Workshop in Nanshi, Shanghai (jointly operated with the Hu family, with assets of 400,000), Yixu Wharf in Nanshi, Shanghai (with assets worth more than 100,000), Xinzhenyuan Smelting Workshop in Suzhou, Yucangxiang Iron Store in Suzhou (with assets of 100,000), Zhengchang Iron Store in Shanghai, and warehouses in Pudong, Zhengchangren Iron Store in Hankou, Shengyuan Oil Factory in Dalian (jointly operated with Ye Hongying), etc. He also owns real estate worth more than 20,000 yuan in Urakami, Nagasaki, Japan, a residence on Qipu Road in Shanghai, more than 3,000 mu of farmland and street houses in the northern part of Wuxi and Zhouxin Town. In recent years, Zhou's business has failed, causing the Shanghai Zhengchang Iron Store and the Hankou Zhengchangren Iron Store to close down one after another. The residence on Qipu Road in Shanghai and the warehouse in Pudong have also been mortgaged. Recently, due to tight liquidity, he has declared bankruptcy, with losses reaching more than 1.5 million. He has entrusted lawyer Sun Zuhong to liquidate the assets. For the debts owed to banks and money shops, the three silk factories, Yuchang, Dingchang, and Shenchang, have been mortgaged, but this is still far from enough. For the debt of more than 200,000 owed to depositors, it is planned to use more than 680 mu of farmland to repay the debt, with each 1,000 yuan yielding about 1.3 mu of farmland. The creditors do not agree, resulting in no result. A creditor group has now been jointly organized to negotiate. However, it is said that Zhou Zhaofu still has 400,000 in deposits in the Bank of China, and another 2,000 mu of farmland, which he claims to have donated to the charity estate.

Jiangyin: Salted Yellow Croaker Refuses to Collect Business Tax 115

Wu Xiacheng, director of the Jiangjing Business Tax Bureau, sent a letter to the Fish and Northern Goods Industry Association, asking them to collect business tax on salted yellow croaker during the current yellow croaker season. The association immediately sent a letter to the Hupu Fish Industry Association in Changshu for consultation. According to the reply, the fish tax and fishery tax have long been exempted by the national government. Salted yellow croaker is collected from the ocean by fishing boats and is not transported for sale, which is different from the nature of business. Moreover, the likin tax has also been abolished long ago. Collecting tax on goods is a disguised business tax that is essentially a restoration of the likin tax, so the collection should be refused.

Jiading: Butcher Gu Jixiang Kills His Father 116

Gu Fengxiang, 65 years old, from Gujiazhai, Zouma Township, Second District, has a son, A Xiang, who is a butcher. On the morning of the 25th, the father and son went to Chenjiahang Town to buy wine and drink together. A Xiang drank wildly and became heavily drunk. After drinking, they still went home together. Fengxiang ordered his family to sun-dry salted fish. A Xiang opposed this and, after a disagreement, A Xiang went to the room and took out the sharp knife he used to slaughter pigs, and stabbed his father in the upper thigh, penetrating his lower abdomen. Fengxiang immediately fainted and soon died. The local village police officer, Meng Zhengu, reported the incident to the Nanxiang Public Security Sub-bureau, which dispatched patrol chief Sun Yuzhen and police officers to investigate and confirm the facts. However, the murder weapon was missing. A Xiang was taken to the sub-bureau and sent to the County Public Security Bureau with a written report. Xue Bingyang, the director of the bureau, interrogated him. A Xiang confessed that he was 46 years old and that he had stabbed his father. He said that he stabbed him in the thigh around 9:00 AM that morning because he was drunk. He was transferred to the county government for detention that evening. The next morning, the hearing officer, Shao Ling, along with police officers, went to the countryside to investigate, verifying that he had been stabbed to death before his death, and ordered the family to prepare the coffin.

The former magistrate of Huaiyin County, Lu Cangeng, was dismissed by the provincial government for failing to effectively recruit workers to dredge the Six Tang Rivers. Qi Yunlong, a counselor of the national government, was appointed to replace him. Qi arrived in Pu at noon the day before yesterday (23rd) and took office yesterday morning (24th). At noon, he returned to the county government.

The Municipal Government Held a Tea Party Yesterday, Mayor Wu Hosted Chinese and Foreign Guests: More Than 800 Cars Arrived on Jiangwan Road, More Than 2,000 Guests Gathered in the Municipal Auditorium, Panchen Arrived at 5 PM, Foreign Guests Rushed to Shake Hands 118

Xinsheng Society reports that Mayor Wu Tiecheng and his wife held a tea party yesterday afternoon at the new municipal government building in the city center, hosting more than 2,000 Chinese and foreign guests, including diplomatic, military, and civilian officials from various countries stationed in Shanghai, as well as leaders from industry and commerce. They enjoyed themselves until late in the evening and then dispersed. The details are as follows:

Traffic Measures 119

The municipal police bureau and the municipal security office dispatched armed police and soldiers around the municipal government in the city center and on Jiangwan Road and Qimei Road to maintain order along the road and dispatched all inspectors to direct traffic at the main roads and in front of and behind the municipal government. From 4:00 PM to 7:00 PM, Jiangwan Road was designated as one-way traffic from south to north, and Qimei Road was designated as one-way traffic from north to south. For the convenience of parking, special marks were prepared and attached to the windshields of the cars. When the cars arrived, they were numbered, and the parking areas in the municipal government square were divided into zones A, B, C, and D for parking in order. In the hall of the new municipal government building, the national flag and the Kuomintang party flag were hung, along with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen. The entrance in front of the government and inside the venue were staffed with receptionists designated by the municipal government. The cloakrooms for men and women were located in the dining room on the lower level. Fresh flowers were placed throughout the municipal government building. The reception room on the first floor was the rest area for newspaper reporters, and the back of the government building was where Chinese and foreign guests boarded their cars when leaving. The military band was located on the west side of the front steps, and the Western band was located on the west corner of the eaves in front of the auditorium.

The Panchen Lama at the Tea Party (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Tea Party Scene 122

After 4:00 PM, guests arrived one after another. The mayor and his wife stood at the door on the east end of the hall and shook hands with each guest as a greeting. Qingdao's Jiaozhou Bay sees imported goods worth over 50 million yuan in national currency annually. Second, Qingdao has only a little over a decade of history since its recovery, during which it has experienced multiple civil wars, and the market has been extremely panicked. Since Mayor Shen took office, he has vigorously promoted industry and developed the market. In recent years, there has been a slight industrial foundation, but compared with the construction technology achievements of major factories in Shanghai, the difference is like heaven and earth. We hope that Shanghai entrepreneurs and technicians will provide more assistance and contributions. Third, the Qingdao port is so good, and the annual consumption is so large, while the inland industrial raw materials are abundant, such as coal, tobacco, peanuts, cowhide, wool, etc., which can be fully supplied. Every bit more of domestic goods sold is a bit more economic rights and interests recovered. We hope that gentlemen of the press will vigorously promote and advocate on behalf of the 400,000 compatriots in Qingdao, to regard Qingdao City as Qingdao for all Chinese people, and to build Qingdao into a Chicago of the United States, or a Manchester of the United Kingdom, and not to regard Qingdao as a 'Switzerland of the East,' a playground park within our country. Furthermore, our delegation believes that the press is the representative of public opinion, and we in the industrial sector especially regard the gentlemen of the press as our nurturers. Qingdao's industry is nascent, and Shanghai newspapers are popular throughout the country and overseas. A single call from a high place will be echoed by ten thousand mountains. Therefore, new industries in Qingdao, such as needle making, gelatin powder production, cowhide glue production, and China Stone Company, rely entirely on sales to have hope of development. The Shanghai press is the mentor of our nascent industry in Qingdao. This is also what our delegation members sincerely pray for."

China Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Hankou Line Increases Flights and Changes Flight Times, Effective from the First of Next Month 131

China Aviation Corporation's Shanghai-Hankou line is now scheduled to increase one flight starting from the first of next month, and at the same time, the flight times will be advanced. The opening hours of the Shanghai-Beiping line will also be changed, and it has been decided to implement it on June 1. The details are as follows:

Increased Flights 132

The company's Shanghai-Hankou line was originally scheduled to fly between Shanghai and Hankou every day from Tuesday to Sunday at 8 am, and arrive separately at 3 pm. Because the business of this line is unusually developed, and passengers and mail are quite crowded, the company, in order to facilitate travel, will also fly normally on Mondays, which were originally rest days, adding a flight to meet the needs. That is, there will be flights every day of the week. The company has decided to implement this from next month (June) 1st.

Earlier Flights 133

In addition, the company, in view of the fact that the summer season is approaching and the weather is getting hotter, will also advance the flight time. The east- and west-bound flights between Shanghai and Hankou will all take off at 7 am every day, and arrive separately at 2:05 pm. At the same time, the flight time of the Shanghai-Beiping line will also be advanced. Every Monday, Wednesday, and Friday, it will depart from Beiping to the south at 6:30 am, and on Tuesday, Thursday, and Saturday, it will depart from Shanghai to the north at 6 am, all arriving at 3:30 pm in the afternoon.

Notice to All Stations 134

After the company decided on the above new regulations, it specifically notified all stations to be informed. The original text reads, "It has been found that from June 1st, the takeoff times of the company's Shanghai-Hankou line and Shanghai-Beiping line aircraft will be advanced (times as above). From the same day, the Shanghai-Hankou line will also be changed to daily flights, with flights on Mondays as well. Accordingly, this letter is to inform you that you should check the station's advertisements and correct them one day in advance, and send the style to us for verification after publication. As for the new timetable, it will be sent separately after it is printed."

Rent Reduction Committee Held a Joint Meeting Yesterday to Schedule Discussions with Representatives of Branch Committees in Various Districts 135

The Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee held its eighth joint meeting of the Executive Design Law at 4 pm yesterday.
