Rent Reduction Promotion Association Contributes Rent Reduction Opinions, Rent Reduction is Closely Related to Prosperity, Specially Sent to the Council for Reference 136

The Rent Reduction Promotion Committee of various groups in this city held a regular meeting at 2 pm yesterday and sent a letter to the Shanghai City Council contributing rent reduction opinions for reference. The details are as follows:

Regular Meeting 137

The Rent Reduction Promotion Committee of various groups in this city held a regular committee meeting at the meeting place at 2 pm yesterday. Nine people attended, including Song Tiren, Yang Xiongzhan, Zhang Gang, Jin Chuxiang, Huang Zhensheng, Zhu Shujian, Qiu Liangyu, Hong Songjiong, and Wang Tingsheng. Qiu Liangyu chaired the meeting to discuss the following cases: (A) Should we notify all industries to deposit the rent in the bank after stopping payment from June? It was decided to submit it to the Executive Committee for discussion. (B) A letter was sent to the council requesting that a copy of the Real Estate Association's opinion be sent to the meeting for research. It was decided to pass it. (C) The nomination of Chen Yongnian as the director of the Organization Section was decided to be handed over to the Executive Committee for selection in order to comply with electoral politics. The meeting adjourned at half past four.

Contributing Opinions 138

The association specially sent a letter to the Shanghai City Council yesterday contributing rent reduction opinions. The original text reads, "The Shanghai rent reduction movement has lasted for four months and has become a prerequisite for Shanghai's prosperity, which has attracted the attention of Chinese and foreign people. Recently, I learned that your council was instructed by the municipal government to discuss the rent issue. The following are the opinions of a humble person for your reference: (1) I believe that housing is one of the four major elements of life and is indispensable to mankind. Nowadays, the prices of clothing and food have fallen greatly compared to before. The reason is related to social economy, that is, the prices of clothing and food change with the social economy, and so does the rent. How was the rent price before the rise of trust transactions? Anyone who has been in Shanghai for a long time can tell. In the past ten years or so, whether it is a resident or a store, although it seems to reluctantly bear this high rent on the surface, the desire for rent reduction has been eager to try. Therefore, the current widespread rent reduction movement can get a hundred responses with one call, and the momentum is rapid, which is enough to show that it is entirely due to accumulation and anger, which is a natural principle among human beings. Since the outbreak of the two major changes of 'September 18' and 'January 28', the social economy has felt extremely uneasy, and Shanghai's prosperity is about to go bankrupt. The so-called large price reductions in the current business market are everywhere. Others such as the agricultural industry summons, the unemployment of workers, and the increasing number of rent arrears cases in the court. Based on this, it is enough to prove that the reduction of rent is closely related to Shanghai's prosperity. This should be noted. (2) I heard that the silver and money industries have deep concerns about the rent reduction issue. The reason is that rent is the interest on real estate. If the rent is reduced, it will inevitably affect the property price. Because many Shanghai houses are mortgaged to the silver and money industries, the trend of rent reduction should not be allowed to grow. However, it is known that this is a rigid view. It should be known that the silver and money industries have never stopped mortgaging silk, rice, yarn, etc. Judging from past facts, after being mortgaged, the prices have fallen miserably, which is often heard. The real estate mortgage is the same. Why worry? The current rent reduction has been forced by the situation. For example, in the distant past, countries such as Germany and Japan had government orders to reduce rent. In recent years, such as our country's rent reduction in Nanjing, the Central Political Council promulgated rent price standards. Our association dares to say that the rent reduction movement is actually beneficial to the society. All industries are members of the society. If the society is beneficial, the mortgaging industry is not without profit. May I ask if the increase in Shanghai's land price is not caused by the general tenants? The tenants gather together in that place, each earning a living, becoming a market, so that the land price increases day by day. The so-called sacrifice by the public to create wealth for individuals is explained in detail in the third lecture of the Principle of People's Livelihood. This should be noted. (3) The rent reduction methods are full of disputes. Some advocate the dominant area theory, some advocate the interest rate theory, and some advocate the house price theory. However, Shanghai has a vast area and densely packed houses. If the above theory is used, it is necessary to start an investigation. However, those who do not understand the overall situation will inevitably conceal the facts. It is difficult to obtain the correct information in a few years. It is appropriate to disturb the society in order to save the society. I have seen that the methods set by the Rent Reduction Committee are based on the year of construction, which is suitable for the urgent needs of the society. This rent reduction movement is originally a last resort, aiming to prosper the market, help each other, unite, and save the crisis together, and there is no hostility between them. This rent reduction method should be transferred to the municipal government for adoption, and the established method should be implemented immediately. This should be noted. In summary, it seems to be practical and easy to implement. I hope you will check it carefully."

Stalemate 140

Even the cigarettes in the warehouse could not be shipped. Yesterday, the workers of the factory continued to strike. The British American tugboat drivers also joined in after the union sent a letter of warning yesterday. The company hired White Russian drivers.

Inside the factory, such as the engine room and furnace room, there were still a few White Russians working, while all others were completely shut down. The company has not made any indication, and the labor side has not sent anyone to negotiate with the company. Both sides are still in a stalemate.

Ministry of Finance Approves the Chamber of Commerce to Reduce Peanut Export Tax for Three Months, Reducing the Original Tax Rate by 60% 148

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously stated in a letter from the Miscellaneous Grain, Oil, and Cake Industry Association that, according to the precedent of Qingdao, it was requested to submit to the Ministry of Finance that all peanut native products exported from Shanghai and transported to various ports in the country be exempted from transit tax for two years. The original text has been seen in previous reports. It is learned that the Ministry of Finance approved the Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that "Received the presentation. It has been checked that peanuts, peanut kernels, and peanut oil shipped from Shanghai have been approved by the Ministry to reduce the originally established export tax rate by 60%, limited to those shipped abroad within three months, that is, from May 26th to August 25th of this year, and the General Taxation Department has been ordered to instruct the customs to comply with it. As for the request to exempt the transit tax, the Ministry has carefully verified it. Peanuts and other products are large Shandong native products, which have a direct relationship with the market in Qingdao, which is different from those transported to Shanghai. Moreover, Shanghai is a collection area for various goods, and the amount of transit peanuts has no significant impact on the prosperity of the market. It cannot be compared with Qingdao, which regards peanut trade as its main business. The request is not approved. Please inform us."

Report of the Red Swastika Society on the Handling of Disaster Relief in Ping'a: 2,500 Hectares of Fertile Land Dredged; Two-Thirds Still Lack Funding 152

The Shanghai General Office of the World Red Swastika Society, due to the severe flooding in Dongping and Dong'a counties in Shandong province last year, specially raised relief funds to be delivered to the Jinan Red Swastika Society for emergency relief. This included dredging the Yellow River estuary in Dong'a, south to Songjiatun in Dongping. They initially raised 7,600 yuan in relief funds. Together with donations from the Shandong Provincial Relief Association and the Northeast Charity Federation, the total amounted to 25,600 yuan. It is now reported that the disaster relief office has submitted a report on the dredging situation: "This Society's disaster relief efforts in Ping'a have been supported by philanthropists from various provinces and the Provincial Relief Association. A large-scale porridge distribution center was set up in the disaster area. Simultaneously, a disaster relief work office was organized to dredge the entire Yellow River estuary. Starting from the Yellow River estuary in Dong'a in the north to Songjiatun in Dongping in the south, the total length is 40 *li*. The northern section, with the highest siltation and the most difficult work, accounts for one-third of the total length. This construction project started with this section. A total of 4,800 to 6,000 laborers from the disaster area were gathered. Each person was paid 13 cents for food daily. Foremen were appointed from the village heads, totaling 357 people, each receiving 23 cents for food daily. It was originally planned that this dangerous section would be completed in 20 days. However, due to two rainfalls and one snowfall, the work was delayed. In addition, the passage of the Liu bandit caused some work delays, extending the project to 32 days before this dangerous section was completed. The total expenditure was 20,421 yuan and 50 cents, with grain contributions from villages valued at over 20,000 yuan, totaling more than 40,000 yuan. Only one-third of the entire project has been completed. This is a significant deviation from the original estimate. According to last winter's estimate by the Dongping County Government, the entire 40 *li* project would only require 20,000 yuan. However, after actual construction began, it was realized that the original estimate was vastly inaccurate. The county government only knew that the work within Dongping was not very difficult, but they were unaware that the section within Dong'a had been severely silted by the Yellow River last autumn, as high as a hill. At this time, appeals for external funds were constant, and villages also struggled to provide grain. Furthermore, with the planting season approaching, work had to be stopped to release the water. It is estimated that around 2,500 hectares of fields have been drained, all planted with barley, interspersed with sorghum. This was only possible due to the support and promotion of various philanthropists. However, in the Ping'a area, more than 5,000 hectares of fields are flooded. This dredging project has only covered one-third, draining half of the flooded fields. If the remaining two-thirds of the southern section can be dredged, all 5,000 hectares of fields can be drained, which is an urgent matter for fundamental disaster relief. According to the project undertaker, the southern section is easier than the northern section. Another 25,000 yuan is needed for completion. Therefore, over the past month, requests have been repeatedly submitted to the Shandong Provincial Government. The result was an approval to continue funding with only 5,000 yuan, which is a significant shortfall, creating the risk of failing at the last hurdle. It is earnestly hoped that philanthropists in Shanghai will continue to provide assistance, so that the entire project can be completed, and all 5,000 hectares of flooded fields can be drained. Not only will the people be spared from drowning, allowing them to join other counties where they can cultivate their land, but also the good deeds of the philanthropists will have boundless merit. Furthermore, the Qinghe Gate is silted up by backflow from the Yellow River every year. If this project is fully completed, it can only guarantee a wheat harvest for two to three years. Continuous dredging every year would be difficult. Now, all village leaders from the disaster area have jointly decided to build a mud dredging boat. During the slack season, the boat will be used for dredging, requiring less effort and achieving greater results. This way, the benevolence of philanthropists will never be wasted. The cost of building the boat is around 80,000 yuan, which will be funded by the harvests from the drained land." This statement was made jointly.

Page 12

Import Tax Evasion of Sugar is Through Smuggling from Dalian: Unloading at Chuanjiacun and Xinggepu, then Transferring to Sailing Vessels to Smuggle into the Interior 159

Since the increase in import duties on foreign sugar, the amount of foreign sugar smuggled into China for sale in the past year has accounted for as much as four-tenths of the total. This has not only caused significant losses in customs revenue but has also severely impacted the business operations of sugar merchants. In order to strictly investigate the source of smuggled sugar, the Tianjin Customs Bureau secretly dispatched special agents to various ports along the coast of North China for secret inspections. After several months of investigation, it was discovered that the source of smuggled sugar was from Chuanjiacun and Xinggepu near Dalian, where foreign sugar was secretly loaded onto ships. After leaving the port, the sugar was transferred to various sailing vessels along the coast, which then privately transported it to Qingdao, Haizhou, and areas outside the Wusongkou estuary, before being smuggled into the interior. In the past year, the amount smuggled into China has reached several million yuan. It is reported that the Dalian authorities in Japan have been notified to closely cooperate in the investigation and crackdown.

Assassination of Wang Delong, Head of the Nanhui Detective Team, Sentenced to Death 160

Zhu Zifan, head of the Nanhui County Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, was shot and killed by Wang Delong (also known as Jinshan) and Chen Delong (also known as Jinshan), both from Pudong, at 8:20 PM on the 11th of this month at the Huibin Inn, No. 13, Lane 369, Guangdong Road. Wang was immediately captured by detectives, while Chen escaped. A pistol and six bullets used in the crime were found on Wang. Li Zhishan, the lawyer of the police station, prosecuted him in the First Special Court for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law. After the interrogation was concluded, Feng Shide, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, announced the verdict in the First Criminal Court yesterday morning. The main verdict was that Wang Delong was sentenced to death for premeditated murder, and the pistol and six bullets were confiscated.

Intense Gunfight as Bandits in Zhabei Resist Arrest; Shopkeepers Peek Through Glass Doors; Tenant's Wife Urgently Reports to Police; One Bandit Killed, Three Captured 161

At 15 Taixing Lane, Baoshan Road in Zhabei, a *shikumen* residence housed Hu Peigeng, a Mi Bo person from the Shunchang Machine Factory on Baotong Road. Qian Shulou had previously rented to Bao Wanglin, a postal worker, and the attic room was occupied by artist Shi Ruihua, all three families residing. Hu was the second landlord. The factory specializes in producing various flashlights. Since the boycott of foreign goods and the promotion of domestic products, business has flourished, resulting in a slight surplus, which attracted the attention of bandits. At 7:30 AM yesterday, while Jiang Dongshi, the maid of the Hu family, was washing a chamber pot at the back door, four bandits wearing long and short gowns suddenly rushed in from the

Back Door 162

They dragged the maid in, pulled out pistols, and warned her to keep quiet. They then herded the men and women of the Hu family into a back room behind the parlor and confined them. They then rummaged through boxes and chests, looting Hu Peigeng's jade ring, gemstone ring, pearl necklace, etc., Shi Ruihua's gold ring, woolen jacket, etc., and Bao Wanglin's leather suitcase, containing sixteen yuan in banknotes, eleven cents in small change. Just as they were about to escape with the stolen goods, the bandits, when entering the door, had not noticed Bao Wanglin's wife buying broad beans from a vendor outside the Hu family's back door. The vendor, through the glass door

Saw the Bandits Enter 163

and informed Bao's wife, who rushed to report the robbery to the police station at No. 44, Fifth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who in turn reported it to District Chief Liang Fuchu, who led Su, a district officer, patrol leader Wang Molin, police officer Gao Chunshan, the entire patrol team, and detective leaders You Hanwen and Lu Hexiang, all fully armed, to the address. Upon seeing the barricaded front and back doors of the house, District Chief Liang immediately ordered the police detectives to surround the residence, while prohibiting other residents from going outside. At the same time, he directed police chief Wang Molin and others to cross the wall from the roof of No. 10 and climb to the sun deck of No. 15. Upon receiving the order, the police detectives all rushed forward with valor. The Mainland News Praises New China One Village; the Environment is Beautiful, Peaceful and Quiet; Equipment is Particularly Complete 166

According to the *Mainland News* of May 24th, the population and houses of Shanghai are increasing day by day. Both old and new residents want to find spacious housing and a quiet environment, but due to the weakness of social economic forces, this has become the most serious problem today. Some people live in the bustling areas of the concessions. Because of the high rents, living in "dovecotes" has become a popular catchphrase. The houses are small, the air is full of smoke and dust, and it is noisy. Some people move to the Shanghai West area because it is more suitable for living conditions, but they suffer from the economic disadvantages. Therefore, the former live in apartments and find it as laborious as climbing mountains to go home, while the latter are too far away, resulting in dusty journeys. The New China Bank pays close attention to the housing problem in Shanghai and attempts to solve the housing problem for the general public with their enthusiasm for serving society. Therefore, they built New China One Village on West Sports Association Road in North Shanghai, with a moderate location, convenient transportation, a superior environment, and economic advantages. New China One Village covers an area of 50 *mu* and is only one *li* away from Hongkou Park. There are main roads connecting it to the Public Concession and the central district of Shanghai. The housing base in the new village has been demarcated. Trees are planted between houses, and there are clean and elegant lawns and gardens. Exquisite and beautiful houses are being built. When the entire project is completed in the future, it will certainly become the best and newest residential area in Shanghai. The purchase method for New China One Village housing is different from that of general real estate companies. The New China Bank knows that the general public lacks the full amount to purchase housing, so it adopts a method of paying in installments. The repayment is included in the rent, so it is very easy and imperceptible. After several years, the housing becomes owned by the resident. The village is surrounded by a beautiful and quiet countryside, without any of the hustle and bustle of the city, but with wide and flat roads and convenient transportation. By private car, it only takes 13 minutes, and by public bus, it only takes 22 minutes to travel between the new village and the Bund. In addition, there is a route to Tiantong'an and Jiangwan, which is where the Songhu Railway passes. Therefore, it is also very convenient for general merchants and women to live there. Although New China One Village is not in the concession area, various facilities are as convenient as in the concession. For example, water and electricity are supplied by the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, and telephone calls can be made directly to the Public Concession and the French Concession. Water and electricity fees and rent are also cheaper than in the concession. In addition, the village is close to the school district, with kindergartens to universities at all levels, such as Shanghai Law School, Chizhi College, Fudan University, Patriotic Girls' School, and Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School. In the future, for the convenience of residents, a small vegetable market and post boxes will be set up. In addition to the above advantages, New China One Village also has a very superior outdoor sports environment. Usually, one can go to Hongkou Park for a walk, swim in the park's swimming pool, or ride horses on the open roads of Jiangwan. It is truly an ideal paradise.

The Case of Liu Shuban and Others Being Accused is Concluded; the Prosecutor's Opinion is Divided into Two Parts; the Debate Was Concluded Yesterday and a Date Was Set for Sentencing 167

The case of Liu Shuban and others, the former directors of the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, being accused of embezzlement and harming the national treasury, was filed by the First Special District Procuratorate of the District Court. Presiding Judge Liu Yugui has repeatedly held court hearings to investigate the case, and the details have been reported in the newspapers many times. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Liu, together with prosecutor Zhong Qing, continued to hear the case of Liang Banxing, the secretary of the Great New Company Preparatory Office. Liang was summoned to court to investigate the circumstances of Zhao Baoshan using part of the commission obtained from the land purchase by the Savings and Remittance Bureau to subscribe to shares of the Great New Company. According to Liang, the company received 23,025 taels of silver from Yang Wutang, Yang Shude, Zhao Huiji, and other four households, equivalent to 30,000 Hong Kong dollars, which was paid by Zhao. He presented the receipt books and share subscription documents as evidence. Judge Liu then questioned Zhao Baoshan and Yang Peichang about the commission and how Zhao purchased shares of the Great New Company. After that, he presented the postal savings rules and repeatedly questioned Liu Shuban and others about the procedures for withdrawing savings with checks. Then, he ordered the debate to begin. Prosecutor Zhong first presented the prosecution's arguments, which were roughly divided into two parts: (1) the commission part of Zhao Baoshan and Yang Peichang, (2) the part of Liu Shuban and others trading in public bonds. Zhong then stated the reasons for the defendants' crimes in the public bond trading event, saying that according to common practice, when banks trade public bonds on behalf of customers, customers should first deposit a margin. However, the defendants' trading of public bonds on behalf of Dai Xunji advanced more than 400,000 yuan without calculating interest. And the 100,000 taels of silver deposited in Liu Jianhou's account, which they claimed to be a margin, was calculated daily. This clearly showed favoritism. In fact, this Dai Xunji account name was the defendant himself, intentionally creating a false name. Judging from his various actions, he has violated Articles 136, 140, and 366 of the Criminal Law. Next, he stated the reasons for the crimes of Zhao Baoshan and others obtaining illegal commissions, saying that the money obtained by the defendants twice for land purchases was 135,000 taels and 29,000 taels respectively. Yang Jianping was given 34,325 taels as a share. According to the custom of real estate transactions, the commission is usually 1% or 1.5% of the property value. However, the property value of Albert Road was 1.2 million taels, and the commission reached 150,000 taels, reaching a level of one-eighth. There has never been such an appalling commission. The defendants colluded with Yang Jianping to inflate the property value and openly share the spoils. The facts are clear and should be judged according to law. Then, the defense lawyers of the defendants, Liu Chongyou, Shi Jiong, Cao Shoulin, Zou Yu, and Liu Shifang, successively defended their clients. The court then ordered a date for sentencing.

Old Servant of the Sheng Xingcun Family Embezzles after 20 Years of Service: Addicted to a Vice and Short on Funds, Steals Valuable Clothes Worth Thousands 168

Sheng Xingcun, formerly a Grand Guardian of the Qing Dynasty, resided at 526 Jing'an Temple Road. His residence was large and expansive, but due to the age of the buildings and the dilapidated walls, the rear buildings were being rebuilt. Therefore, all important chests and belongings of his descendants were placed in one room, named the storage room. It was sealed and entrusted to his servant, Ruan Ronggen, to guard. Ruan, a native of Anhui, was employed by Sheng's second concubine and had served for 20 years. He was usually very honest and without any vices. However, recently, due to a certain addiction, he became short on funds. After much deliberation, he took a risk. On the 22nd of this month, at 2:30 AM, before dawn, when all was quiet, he colluded with a relative, identified as Jia, to open the clothes chests in the storage room. They selected two chests of important clothes, valued at 9,554 yuan, and secretly stole them. They hired rickshaws to take them to a friend's place, planning to pawn them later. The matter was discovered by the Sheng residence when they noticed the seal on the chests had been torn. Upon closer inspection, they realized that clothes worth thousands of yuan had vanished. At the time, they did not know who had stolen them, and Ruan remained calm, continuing his duties as usual. Subsequently, Huang Dazhong, representing the Sheng residence, reported the situation to the Xinzha Police Station. The station immediately dispatched Chinese Detective Tang Jian, Yao Yuanlong, Detective Lu Gendi, Jiang Juwu, Constable Xia Yeshan, and foreign detective Qijasheng. After days of detailed investigation, they found Ruan Ronggen, a servant of the Sheng residence, to be suspicious and evasive. They took Ruan to the police station for questioning yesterday. Ruan confessed to the theft and led the Chinese and foreign detectives to 334 Meibai Ke Road and 97 Jin Shenfu Road in the French Concession, where they arrested two other suspects, Dou Guanghua and Yin Bengen. They also recovered most of the stolen goods, clothing worth over 7,700 yuan, and took them to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District. The police station's lawyer, Gan Jingguang, presented the case and requested a postponement to investigate and recover the remaining stolen goods. Judge Wu Zehan briefly questioned the defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody separately, pending further investigation.

### Swearing to Be Shot: Shen Mingming Claims Frame-up by Detective Xu Guirong, but Sentenced to Two Years Imprisonment Due to Evidence 169

Shen Mingming, a local resident of a bungalow with no number on Ninghe Road, Yangshupu, was around 70 years old and a local bailiff with a well-to-do family. Recently, the Narcotics Department detective Xu Guirong discovered that he was selling red pills. Xu reported this to the foreign detective chief Bai Pu, who, on the morning before yesterday at about 10:00 AM, took a court search warrant and secretly went to arrest Shen at his residence. They found a "double horn" mark on his person, a sign used by informants to buy pills. In an old basket of clothes on a long bench under the eaves of the house, they found four packets of red pills, estimated to be several thousand. In the bedroom, they found an opium lamp. They took everything to the Yangshupu Police Station, and the captain ordered them to be detained. The next morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District. The Public Works Bureau lawyer Wang Yuetang stated that on the 16th and 17th of this month, Detective Xu sent informants to the defendant's residence, buying two small packets of pills for two jiao each time. The third time, he used a foreign knife to mark a "double horn" on a coin as a secret sign, then bought another small packet. Chinese and foreign detectives then entered the house and arrested Shen. He is now being prosecuted under Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. The seized evidence included a "double horn" coin, seven packets of red pills of various sizes, and an opium lamp. Chinese and foreign detectives then reported the details of the arrest. When questioned, the defendant said he never sold red pills, had known Detective Xu for years, and claimed Xu framed him because of a past grievance. Shen alleged that Xu sent a henchman to invite him out for tea twice that morning, but he declined. While Shen was absent, Xu secretly put the red pills in the basket. Shen also claimed the "double horn" mark found on his person was stuffed into his pocket during the arrest and that the opium lamp was from a past illness. Shen stated he would rather be shot than admit to selling red pills. Detective Xu denied the defendant's claims. Wu Sijin, a Suzhou woman and Shen's tenant of over ten years, testified that he did not sell red pills. Zhang Defa, a Haizhou native and police informant, testified that he had bought small packets of red pills from Shen three times for two jiao each, and that Shen personally delivered them to him. Judge Xiao Xiefen, considering the evidence conclusive, sentenced Shen Mingming to two years' imprisonment and a fine of 1,000 yuan. The evidence was confiscated. The defendant's lawyer appealed and requested bail, but the court rejected the guarantee offered by dozens of neighboring shopkeepers and ordered Shen to remain in custody.

Japanese University Students Gambling Madly at Mahjong: Classrooms Used as Gambling Dens, Thugs Extorting Money 170

According to the Tokyo Kokumin Shimbun of the 18th, the recent issues of students frequenting dance halls and the mahjong gambling incidents involving students from Tokyo University and Keio University are on the rise. The disruption of school discipline has become a problem among informed people. Surprisingly, students from Rikkyo University, an institution known for its exceptional reputation and operated by a missionary group, have been continuously gambling at mahjong in classrooms. The hidden secrets within are particularly alarming. More than 20 students, including Shiro Yamagishi, often used chips instead of cash (five or ten sen). Since February of this year, they have taken advantage of teachers' absences or breaks to gamble wildly at mahjong in classrooms. Classmates kept watch outside the door to prevent anyone from finding out. As a result, not only was the content unknown to outsiders, but it was also difficult for school authorities to discover their secret. Later, as time passed, a thug named Takagi, whose younger brother was also a thug, began visiting the school from late April, insisting on meeting with these students. He threatened them, demanding twenty yuan per person as a "longevity fee," or he would report them to the police. Takagi extorted several hundred yuan in blackmail money. However, feeling increasingly unsafe, he fled into hiding. As a result, the truth of the case gradually came to light.

Both Railway Bureaus Act as Agents for Collecting MOGANSHAN Joint Transportation Vehicle and Sedan Chair Surcharges; Agreed-Upon Methods Extended for One Year 172

The joint transportation vehicle and sedan chair surcharge collection method for Moganshan, previously agreed upon by the two Railway Bureaus with the Zhejiang Provincial Highway Administration and the Moganshan Management Office, generally stipulated that the Highway Administration and the Railway Bureau would act as agents for the Moganshan Management Bureau in collecting joint transportation passenger vehicle and sedan chair surcharges. The surcharge rates were: (A) Vehicle Surcharge: First, second, and third-class passengers, adults, were charged 2 jiao per person; children (age determined by railway regulations) were charged 1 jiao per person; (B) Sedan Chair Surcharge: Sedan chair carriers were charged 1 jiao per person. Those purchasing round-trip tickets were charged double the above rates. The effective period of this method was originally scheduled to end at the end of the 22nd year. The Railway Bureau intended to continue the method for another year after the expiration date and sent letters to the Railway Bureau for their agreement. The Railway Bureau believed that this agreement would be beneficial to the overall construction of the mountain and should be supported. However, the phrase "Railway Bureau by the Hangzhou Rolling Stock Section Chief" in Article 5 of the agreement should be changed to "Railway Bureau by the Hangzhou-Jiazhaba Rolling Stock Section Chief or the Moganshan Railway Hotel Manager" to comply with the Railway's current organizational structure. Furthermore, when railway employees travel from Hangzhou to Moganshan or from the mountain to Hangzhou, the Section Chief or Hotel Manager would provide a written certificate to exempt them from paying the vehicle and sedan chair surcharges. The matter has already been communicated and related departments have been instructed to comply.

Tuberculosis Prevention Work in the Health Movement: The China Anti-Tuberculosis Association Formulates an Outline 175

The 13th Shanghai Health Movement Congress will begin on the 19th of next month. The tuberculosis prevention work will be carried out by the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association. The Association has finalized the outline for tuberculosis prevention work in the Health Movement Congress as follows:

Publicity The Association, in order to raise public awareness of tuberculosis prevention, will have its members organize a costumed propaganda team to participate in performances in public places. It will also give a large-scale tuberculosis prevention lecture in the East, South, West, and North districts of the city. Workers and their families are welcome to attend to gain common knowledge on tuberculosis prevention. It is also planned to request all parks in the city to be open, and the Association will post various pictures, slogans, and other promotional materials in each park to achieve widespread publicity.

Practical Work In addition to publicity, the Association plans to conduct temporary business during the Congress. The Association will designate four elementary schools in the East, West, South, and North districts of the city to carry out tuberculin tests. It will also contact well-known hospitals in the city to provide free tuberculosis examinations for citizens during the Congress. X-rays will also be available at half price. All physicians registered with the Municipal Health Bureau should also charge half price for tuberculosis examinations during the Congress.

Xie Shan Commits Suicide by Poisoning: In a Hongkou Apartment, He Takes Poison: The Suicide Note Was Addressed to Chen Rutian: |Notes on the Back of a Photo of Him With a Woman| 180

Around noon the day before yesterday, a middle-aged man, speaking Cantonese and wearing a grey-blue silk spring gown and a grey felt hat, opened room number two in the Jiande Apartment at 737 North Sichuan Road. He was about thirty years old, with a haggard face and faltering steps. He claimed to be Li Dechen, a 29-year-old timber merchant from Guangdong. He paid a rent of two yuan. After the tea servant brought tea and water and left, he closed the door tightly. Around 5:00 PM, he opened the door and called the tea servant to buy him food. Around 7:00 PM in the evening, he ordered a bowl of noodles, ate it, and then closed the door and went to sleep. Unexpectedly, around midnight, there was a groaning sound in the room. The tea servants suspected something was wrong and rushed to knock on the door. After a long time with no response, they reported to the accounting office. They used a wooden ladder and a flashlight to look through the window and saw the guest lying stiffly in bed, motionless. Realizing something was wrong, they climbed in through the balcony, turned on the lights, and saw him foaming at the mouth, barely breathing. They reported to the first section of the fifth district and notified the fire brigade to dispatch a fire engine to take him to the Red Cross Hospital for treatment. However, he had taken too much poison and died at around 4:00 AM yesterday morning. The police station sent officers to investigate and reported to the court for an autopsy yesterday morning. Two suicide notes were found on the pillow, one addressed to the apartment, asking them to notify his friend Chen Rutian to handle the funeral. The other was addressed to Chen Rutian, stating, "Last night, I ate at Tan Manji and came out. I went to a Hongkou hotel to commit suicide by poisoning. Because I bought too little opium, only six jiao worth, I suffered all night and didn't die. Today, I took poison and bought one yuan worth of opium, which should kill me," signed Xie Xiushan. Therefore, the deceased's real name was Xie Xiushan. He had first attempted suicide by poisoning at a Hongkou hotel, and then moved to the Hongkou Apartment to try again. The reason for the suicide is unknown. A photo was found on the deceased, a photo of the deceased and a female companion, with the words "Please Chen Rutian publish this photo to invite someone to claim the body" on the back. The first section of the fifth district is investigating the person Chen Rutian, hoping to find the truth.

The Shanghai Municipal History Museum Publishes a Compilation of Periodicals 184

The Shanghai Municipal History Museum, with the spirit of working hard together, is engaged in the compilation of the city's general history. In order to solicit advice from scholars and public criticism, it has printed several drafts on a quarterly basis and published a periodical to distribute to all sectors. Not only is the museum's work specifically demonstrated by the periodical, but also its attitude of painstaking research and lack of perfunctoriness are also spread to the academic community. In a very short period of time, the world has not only been able to anticipate that the Shanghai Municipal History will open a new era in China's local history, but it has also confirmed that the museum is one of China's important academic institutions. However, due to financial constraints, the museum's periodicals have a very limited print run and have not been distributed widely. The museum is very sorry that it cannot meet the demands of those who have repeatedly requested them. The museum has now taken advantage of the publication of the periodical for a full year to re-examine it in detail and reprint 300 copies, which are compiled into a book to meet the needs. The compilation contains a total of more than 1,100 years and about 700,000 words. All departments of Shanghai, including the origin of the city, the public concession, the French concession, diplomacy, finance, academic arts, industry, and social undertakings, have historical records ranging from tens of thousands to more than one hundred thousand words. It is an essential resource for those interested in studying Shanghai and understanding the important history of China in the last hundred years. The compilation costs five yuan per book, plus one yuan for postage for other places. Those who need it can contact the museum directly at 291 Saposai Road, Shanghai, to purchase it to avoid missing the opportunity again.

The Chinese Women's Temperance Union held a banquet at the Hong Kong Road Bankers Association at noon yesterday to say farewell to Ms. Yang Meizhen, the representative attending the International Women's Temperance Union Conference. After the conference, she plans to study in the United States and will also investigate the lives of women internationally for about two years.

Car Driver Appeals for Lighter Sentence in Fatal Car Accident Case 188

Car driver Gao Chunsheng, on March 22nd of this year, at approximately 9:00 AM, drove a privately-owned car with the license plate number 892 belonging to Russian doctor Mai Qi (transliteration) from Xiafei Road in the French Concession eastward to the tram stop at the intersection of Luban Road. Due to the driver's negligence, he struck Wang Mo (courtesy name Bingqing), a Shaoxing native who was the chief of the Document Section of the Ministry of Finance's Tax Affairs Department, causing his death. The French police department's traffic division arrested Gao and handed him over to the Second Special District Local Court for public prosecution. The victim's family also filed a civil suit, seeking damages of 30,000 yuan. The initial trial sentenced Gao to three years in prison and ordered him to compensate the victim's family with 5,000 foreign yuan. Gao, dissatisfied with the original verdict, appealed to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The court held a hearing the other day. In the private prosecution part, a settlement was reached in court for 2,600 yuan, to be paid in three installments. The public prosecution part was declared closed, pending the pronouncement of the verdict. The above situation has been recorded in previous reports. Yesterday, Judge Guo, together with Assessors Sun and Fan, held a hearing and announced the verdict. The main text of the original judgment was revoked, and Gao Chunsheng was sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for causing death due to negligence in his business. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day, which is half of the original sentence. It is reported that Gao still expressed dissatisfaction and intended to appeal to the Supreme Court for a third trial, hoping to escape punishment.

Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center Publishes "Today's Rural Movement" 189

The Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center has been making tireless contributions to publishing. Now, the first research report of the center, "China's Rural Movement Today," has been published. The book was written by Kong Xuexiong, a researcher at the center, and describes the rural movements in various parts of the country over the past ten years in great detail. The experimental movements in various places, such as Ding County, Zouping, and Zhenping, are all described in a detailed and analytical manner. The development of various rural construction theories, such as village governance theory, rural education, and local autonomy, is also discussed in a systematic manner. All the descriptions are based on actual investigations and are by no means empty talk. At a time when rural revitalization is being highly promoted, this book is the best reference material for both those who are engaged in practical work in the countryside and researchers of rural issues. The content includes a general discussion of the meaning and conditions of the rural movement, rural construction in Shandong, the Ding County experiment of the China Association for Promoting Mass Education, rural improvement projects and mass education in Jiangsu, the Zhenping militia and autonomy in the bandit areas, the rural credit cooperative business in Hebei, the movement from Xiaozhuang School to industrial study groups, and the Xiaoshan Eastern Township autonomy under Party-led administration. All of these are extremely brilliant. Finally, it summarizes the gains and losses of the work in various places and his personal opinions. The general trend of the rural reconstruction movement in China in recent years, as well as those that can be called representative works, are roughly covered without omission. In addition, there is a preface by Mr. Sun Zhesheng and three appendices, including a survey of the national rural improvement business and a list of rural activists, which are also relatively complete. The entire book has more than 240,000 words, bound in a thick volume, and is priced at 1.50 yuan. It is sold at major bookstores such as the Commercial Press, the Author's Bookstore, and the Modern Bookstore. The issuing office is the Zhongshan Cultural and Educational Center on Fuxu Road in Shanghai.

After the "Jing'an" Steamer is Detained, Private Shipping Industry Holds Meeting to Assist, Resolves to Petition the Government for Release 190

The "Jing'an" steamer of the Sanbei Steamboat Company, which operates on the Shanghai-Hankou route, has been detained for more than 40 days since Yu Shicheng accused it of sinking a Fuzhou small steamer and requested the court to seize it, resulting in huge losses. Furthermore, Yu Qiaqing, the manager of the company, believes that the sinking of the Fuzhou small steamer was not caused by the "Jing'an" steamer at all. The Shanghai Maritime Administration's Ship Collision Dispute Handling Committee conducted a detailed investigation of the case, summoned witnesses and evidence, and determined that it was not the "Jing'an" steamer that collided. Now, the private shipping companies, believing that the "Jing'an" steamer has been unjustly detained, are outraged and fear that everyone will be in danger in the future. They have decided to convene a meeting within the next few days to discuss petitioning the government for its release, and they will not stop until their goal is achieved.

Zhang Shunsheng Destroys Agreed-Upon Prices and Dares to Wield a Chisel to Commit Assault, Sentenced to Seven Months in Prison 191

Zhang Shunsheng from Changzhou opened a workshop for manufacturing rubber stamps and ox horn handles at No. 100 Ziyou Lane, Guangdong Road. Zhang Bingqing also opened the Yongxing Bookstore on Wangping Street. In the past, due to business competition, they had invited their colleagues to discuss and unify the price, with each ox horn handle priced at 1.2 jiao foreign currency, and no discounts were allowed. However, Zhang Shunsheng recently suddenly reduced the price to 7.7 li, which is 3.5 li less than the agreed-upon price. Zhang Bingqing learned of this and, at 8:20 PM last night, led his shop assistants Liu Xingsheng and Li Delin to Zhang Shunsheng's place to reason with him and invite him to a teahouse for judgment. Unexpectedly, Zhang Shunsheng, knowing that he was at fault, used a working chisel to stab Bingqing's thigh and both arms five times in a row, all the way through, immediately injuring him and causing him to fall to the ground. Liu Xingsheng immediately stepped forward to stop him and was also stabbed in the eyebrow and chest. At that time, Zhang Shunsheng knew that he had caused a disaster and begged Liu and Zhang not to report to the police, promising to send them to the hospital for treatment, with the medical expenses being borne by him. He then took Liu and Zhang to Renji Hospital for treatment. The hospital telegraphed the Laozha Police Station, and Detective Wang Yifei went to arrest Zhang Shunsheng and detain him in the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Criminal Court of the First Special District. Police lawyer Li Zhishan stated the case and prosecuted him under Article 294 of the Criminal Law. According to Zhang Bingqing's statement of the situation at the time, he claimed, "I have fainted three times since being stabbed yesterday and the pain is unbearable." The defendant, when questioned, claimed that he was slapped in the face by the plaintiffs and his front teeth were loosened, causing him to become confused and cause this great disaster. Judge Feng Shide verified the confession and sentenced Zhang Shunsheng to seven months of imprisonment for injuring someone using a method sufficient to cause serious injury.

▲Zhao Anzhi Revises Painting Fee. He excels in figures, landscapes, flowers, birds, grasses, and insects. He combines the strengths of various masters and melts them into one. He often amuses himself with painting in his spare time from reading, which is truly rare. His small pieces of paper are treasured like precious jewels. In the spring of the 18th year of the Republic of China, his works were specially invited to the National Art Exhibition and received great praise at home and abroad. In the winter of the 19th year, he won a gold medal at the Li Anqi International Exposition, and his name became known overseas. In the spring of the 22nd year, he responded to the Chicago Exposition and was highly praised by the people there. In the spring of the 23rd year, he responded to the invitation of the Sino-German Painting Exhibition, and many of his works were purchased. In June of the same year, the Chicago Exposition reopened and he received a letter requesting him to continue to exhibit his works. His barbarian bows and clothing can be compared to the best. Recently, he has been painting Bodhisattvas, Buddha statues, and Arhats, copying the true works of the Tang and Song Dynasties, which are brilliant, solemn, and deeply inspired. His art is advanced in the way. Cai Yuanpei, Wen Lanting, Dong Shoujin, Wang Yiting, Chu Minyi, Wu Hufan, and others have revised Zhao's painting fee. Those who love calligraphy and painting can contact Tan Jinzhang at the business department of the Shen Bao newspaper.

Questions and Answers for Studying During the Day

Knowledge Required for Work: Reading Guidance... 198

I sincerely request some guidance from you for the knowledge required for my work.

My current position is equivalent to that of a librarian, but with a different title. Therefore, I would like to acquire some knowledge about "statistics," "classification," and "cataloging." I don't know if there are any books on these subjects? Which bookstore publishes them? Please give me a detailed answer, sir.

Also, in my spare time, I would like to study some printing technology. I don't know if there are any magazines or books in China that specialize in printing? Please indicate this as well, I would be very grateful!

丨Letter from Xu Zhusan丨

Knowledge required for work is the most practical knowledge. I think naturally Xu is not alone in needing such knowledge. Social guidance in this area has always been neglected. This column has rarely discussed such questions before, but it is not because we have not noticed it. It is because such ordinary questions are actually the most difficult to answer. Previously, we did not find people with expertise in many areas. For example, a varnish maker asked us some chemical questions, and we could not find anyone to answer them. Therefore, we often could not satisfy the readers' wishes. This time, Xu is asking about the knowledge of library science, which is akin to asking our own family.

However, before we discuss the knowledge of the practical questions related to the needs of the business, we must first understand what kind of department his work is in. What difficulties are encountered at the specific work? What are its specific contents and scope? If there is no boundary, our answer has no way to start.

It seems that Xu's question is rather vague, general, and abstract. Although he talked about "statistics," "classification," and "cataloging" and other issues, he did not point out any narrow range of these problems. Here, we can only write about the general library science theory to the best of our ability...

First, classification is the most cumbersome task in the library, and that is generally recognized. The meaning of book classification is generally to "put things of the same nature together". However, this sentence, at first glance, seems very clear in meaning, and there is no difficulty, but in fact, it is often the case that a book has to be listed in two or three or more categories. When encountering such divergence and ambiguity, it often takes a lot of time to think hard, so doing this work sometimes can really make people impatient, because you can't get the most appropriate category: but sometimes you will feel happy and interesting, although that's the way it is said, There are always principles and experiences to refer to in dealing with any matter. Let us mention three points as follows (1) Since there is no absolute scientific classification in book classification, then we can take theory as the basis on one hand, but take facts as the premise on the other hand. It is the combination and interpenetration of these two. The only thing we have to do is to make the books feel convenient to take and place in operation, then sacrificing a little theoretical law is possible. For example, in natural science, there is electricity and electrical engineering in applied technology, the former is about electricity in principle of natural science; the latter is about the technology of electrical engineering in applied technology, according to the theory, the two examples mentioned above should be given two categories, but if there are not many collections, at the same time, for the reference of a certain problem and to avoid scattering, it is also reasonable to summarize them in one category. (2) When determining the category of each book, try to take the highest meaning. For example, if there is a book about the "May 30th Incident", this book can be divided into the issue of Sino-Japanese and Sino-British diplomacy, and it can also be divided into modern Chinese history, but it is not as great as dividing it into the meaning of the Chinese national liberation and revolutionary movement. (3) The order of classification has a considerable significance, and this point should also be based on the laws of theory as much as possible. For example, if there are several books about the records of social thought history, it is necessary to consider the order of occurrence and not reverse the order.

The three items mentioned above belong to the general and important arguments of the classification method. At the same time, it is too short to write about the theory in this area here. It is impossible to list them in detail. As for the question of which method to use for classification, we generally agree with the Dewey Decimal System because of its flexibility. If the library is small and there are not many books, you only need to use the outline. If the scale is large and there are many books, you can use both the outline and the outline. If the outline is still not enough, you can add decimal points.

(2) Cataloging is a more complete work of the library after classification. If the library has a complete catalog, readers can use the catalog to guide them to retrieve the information they want in their hearts. However, this cataloging is a very practical work and must be understood through practice. Moreover, the cataloging depends entirely on the needs and complexity of the library to determine the work. Some libraries only produce a book title catalog. Some libraries also have author catalogs, title catalogs, classification catalogs, and even dictionary-style catalogs, but usually libraries have book title and author catalogs. As for the methods of cataloging, there are many rules that are difficult to list in fact. Fortunately, there are special books for introduction below, so I will not repeat them here.

(3) Regarding the issue of statistics, we also think that it is almost the same situation as cataloging, that is, how to count the materials generated in the business that Xu has put forward, which depends entirely on the actual needs. As for the principles and methods of statistics, the following books can be used as a reference.

(4) Regarding magazines and books specializing in printing, I have not heard of them in China. Recently, the Commercial Press Publishing Weekly has a column "Printing Knowledge" in Issue 75, which is also worth reading. Furthermore, today's newspaper reported that the library published a book on modern printing technology, priced at 4 jiao. We made a special trip to purchase and read it. It is said that it is still their first work. This little thing may slightly fill your desire for printing knowledge in case.

The 5th Shanghai People's Amateur Games are scheduled to be held today at the Municipal No. 1 Public Sports Field. Sports will begin at 7:30 AM, and all athletes and referees must be present on time. The opening ceremony will be held at 8:00 AM, with Mayor Wu personally delivering the opening address. The preliminary rounds for the 800 meters, 200 meters, and 3,000 meters were completed yesterday in the fading light. Those who score points in this sports event will be awarded a medal at any time. The St. John's, Jiaotong, Soochow, and Aurora University Track and Field Meet was held yesterday afternoon starting at 2:00 PM at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui. Northern China Athletes for the Far Eastern Championship Departed Hong Kong Yesterday Morning; South China Football Team Lost to Western Union 3-0 Yesterday 213

(Hong Kong, 26th) The Northern China athletes for the Far Eastern Championship departed Hong Kong on the President Jackson yesterday morning. Only the Southern China athletes remain in the football team. They played against Western Union at the South China Stadium at 5:30 PM, and Western Union won 3-0.

(Central News Agency, Hong Kong, 26th) The Far Eastern Championship delegation of over 80 people, led by Wang Zhengting, departed Hong Kong on the original Jackson ship at 8:00 AM on the 26th. Representatives from various groups came to the port to see them off.

(Central News Agency, Hong Kong, 26th) The Far Eastern Championship football delegation played a friendly match against Western Union at the Hong Kong Club Stadium at 5:30 PM on the 26th. Li Huitang and Feng Jingxiang did not play due to other commitments, which significantly weakened the team. The players were also fatigued from the journey, leading to poor coordination. As a result, Western Union won 3-0.

Guangdong Champion in Ping Pong Xiangbin Cup; Jiande Absent from the Final 217

The 7th Ping Pong Xiangbin Cup was held as scheduled last night at the Meifeng Ping Pong Room. The chairman of the cup competition staff association, considering the previous request for postponement of the final, which had a major impact, specifically sent letters to both Guangdong and Jiande teams, stating that if they were absent from the final, they would be dealt with according to Article 7, Item 9 of the cup competition rules, "withdrawal midway." Unexpectedly, three hours before the final, letters were received from both teams, requesting postponement of the match, the reason being a conflict with the Chinese team's preliminary selection time." (According to the so-called Chinese team preliminary selection, it is said to be in preparation for the "Far Eastern Sino-Japanese Ping Pong Competition" to be held next month). The association immediately replied, saying that all matters had been arranged long ago, and it was difficult to comply with the request for postponement. It also pointed out that now that the Far Eastern Games have been illegally dissolved, even the Sino-Japanese tennis exhibition match has been canceled, so why bother with this Ping Pong? Therefore, it hoped that they would still attend on time. When the final arrived, the Guangdong team, as expected, understood the greater good and attended in full, while the Jiande team, except for the team captain Lu Zhongqiu, was absent. Therefore, the referee Zhou Weixin announced that Jiande had forfeited, and the representative of the cup competition staff association explained the situation, stating that it should be treated as a withdrawal midway. All of their competition results in this session will be canceled. As a result, this year's championship was won by the Guangdong team. The runners-up were promoted in turn to be tied between the Tianma and Meifeng teams, and each was presented with a flag for encouragement. The awards were presented by Ms. Shi Shuming, and finally, everyone dispersed after enjoying a banquet of refreshments.

Chinese Ping Pong Association Rejects Japanese Team's Visit to Shanghai for Competition; Preliminary Selection Will Still Be Held as Scheduled 218

The Shanghai Chinese Ping Pong Association previously decided to hold the Chinese team preliminary selection, starting on the evening of the 23rd of this month, to select talented players in preparation for the Sino-Japanese International Ping Pong Championship, which will be held in Shanghai, China, in early June. However, since the Far Eastern Games were destroyed by the Japanese, people throughout the country have been indignant. The Japanese side, in order to fulfill its long-cherished wish to participate in the so-called East Asian Amateur Sports Association illegally, used its ghost tricks, which are not worth the ridicule of discerning people. It is now understood that the association, in view of the Japanese side's unreasonable destruction of the Far Eastern Games, is deeply indignant and has decided to send a telegram to Japan rejecting the visit to Shanghai for the competition. As for the preliminary selection of the Chinese team, as it is an association matter that the association should handle, it will still be held as scheduled to assess the players' skills.

Tenth Anniversary of the Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School 221

▲ Sports Performance…To Be Held Tonight

The Tenth Anniversary Celebration of the Southeast Women's Physical Education Normal School in Jiangwan will feature a sports performance tonight (the 27th). The program is extensive, and the performances are novel. All the clothing and accessories are made by the school's students themselves, so preparations have been extremely busy in recent days. In addition, the school's performance will feature a variety of dances, so it will be held in the evening. Various colored lights have been installed in the school's track and field, and an archway has been built in front of the gate. The school also feared that it would be inconvenient for guests to travel back and forth late at night, so it contacted the China General Omnibus Company and obtained approval for Route 4 buses to run until 12:00 AM.

Committee for the Design of Labor Education of the Ministries of Industry and Education 225

▲Passes resolution to request the establishment of experimental labor education zones

(Nanjing, 26th) The Committee for the Design of Labor Education of the Ministries of Industry and Education held a meeting on the 25th. The most important resolution was to petition the Ministries of Industry and Education to plan and establish experimental labor education zones, designating Shanghai, Wuxi, Qingdao, Tianjin, Hankou, and other locations for pilot programs to facilitate the implementation of labor education. This proposal was discussed at length, and ultimately passed as is, along with a revised draft of the organizational charter for experimental labor education zones under the Ministry of Industry. Other resolutions, such as establishing labor education implementation committees in industrially developed areas, petitioning the Ministries of Industry and Education to organize a committee for compiling labor education materials, petitioning the Ministries of Industry and Education to send responsible personnel to inspect, guide, and supervise designated experimental labor education zones, urging social education institutions in cities to focus on labor education and establish dedicated labor education implementation agencies, and editing and publishing labor songs, were also revised and passed.

Junior High School Student Drowns While Swimming at Provincial Nanjing Middle School 227

Zhou Gao, a 19-year-old student in the A group of the third grade of junior high school at Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Middle School, a native of Jiangning County, Jiangsu Province, went to exercise on the playground as usual after class at 4:00 PM on the 25th of this month. (The school's playground is outside the perimeter wall, which is very low and has recently been knocked down by outsiders, making it easy to cross.) When the self-study class started at 7:00 PM, the student was missing. While searching for him, Chen Ju and other students from Anhui Middle School reported to the school that Zhou Gao had been swimming in the swimming pool near the Jiulong Bridge outside Tongji Gate and suddenly disappeared. Upon hearing this, the junior high school director immediately instructed the resident tutor and class advisor Zhou Zhongchen, physical education teacher Li Kehang, and four other faculty members to rush to the scene. At the same time, they reported to the principal (at the first campus). After the class advisor and others arrived at Jiulong Bridge, they hired local security guard Wang Hong to find someone to dredge the pool. After about half an hour, they pulled the student ashore. His limbs were stiff and his abdomen was sunken. Li Kehang tried artificial respiration, but it was ineffective. They instructed the local security guard to watch the body and dispatched four school workers to guard the site. The principal, upon hearing the news, went to the second campus and sent someone with a letter to inform the student's parents in Xijiao Village, Chunhua Town, outside Tongji Gate. Three supervisors from the Provincial Department of Education happened to be in Nanjing for inspection and were staying at the second campus. They were informed of the situation and reported to the provincial supervisors, and also telegraphed the Department of Education. Separately, they reported to the 9th Police Substation and requested the Jiangning District Court to send personnel for an autopsy.

May this sunshine shine on boys and girls wherever they are, reduce their worries and encourage them with ever-increasing enthusiasm to undertake the great mission of goodwill and peace among all mankind. May these modest congratulations trigger a continuous message of goodwill that circles the world on Children's Goodwill Day.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

How Can Students Practice the New Life Movement? 235

— Bo Zhen

"New Life, New Life." What a fashionable slogan. The purpose of the New Life Movement is to build the nation and revive the nation! To improve the knowledge and morality of the people! To make the general public's clothing, food, housing, and transportation orderly, clean, simple, and plain. In accordance with propriety, righteousness, integrity, and a sense of shame! It can be seen that the purpose of the New Life Movement is so significant! How important!

We students are the future masters of the country, and the responsibility of saving the country rests on our shoulders. We are the vanguard of practicing the New Life Movement, so we should understand how to practice the New Life Movement.

The most important ones are probably the following two points:

(1) Rules: We must abide by the rules as human beings, so there is also a rule in the New Life Movement's rules. When you see someone in the morning, you should say "Good morning." When parting, say "Goodbye." As the saying goes, "It doesn't cost anything to greet people, just roll your tongue." When eating, do not be rude. Walk on the left. There are many rules, too many to list.

(2) Cleanliness: Cleanliness is the key to longevity, so there is also a cleanliness rule in the New Life Movement. Clothes should be washed often, windows should be opened often, nails should be trimmed often, and hair should be combed often.

I think someone must say: "It is so difficult and troublesome to implement so many rules one by one." In fact, what is so difficult about this? Why be a person who is afraid of trouble? Just implement one or two rules every day, and in a month or two, you will have implemented the New Life Movement.

Little friends, I think you are really not afraid of difficulties and troubles.

The Story of May 236

— Ding He

One evening in May, when Yingdi and Lanmei were fighting for a piece of cake, Dad came back from outside. When they saw Dad, they threw away the cake and went up to call Dad.

Dad just smiled at them and sat down on a chair next to them. Then, he asked them to sit aside and also asked me to sit aside.

Dad first opened his mouth and asked his younger brother what month it was now.

Yingdi quickly said "May." Dad then asked Lanmei, and Lanmei also quickly said "May." Dad asked me again.

"May is May, but we should call it National Humiliation Month."

After I finished speaking, Dad nodded and said, "Very correct." But Yingdi and Lanmei became strange. At this time, Dad sighed and said:

"Just remembering it, not thinking about washing away the humiliation, is no longer what we should do. You, not only do you not think about washing away the humiliation, but you don't even remember it."

So Yingdi and Lanmei cried. At this time, Dad laughed again and told them the story of May from beginning to end, in detail.

After Dad finished telling the story of May, Yingdi said: "We want to unite the children of China, rise up together to wash away the humiliation, rise up together to wash away the humiliation."

Sibling Rivalry 237

— Hu Yunwu

One day, hands and feet argued about who was more noble and lowly. The hand scolded the foot and said, "There is nothing more lowly than your 'foot' in the world. Why? First, your soles are always stepping on the ground, never seeing the light of day. Second, your appearance, 'foot', if you were to pick it up and show it to people, people would scold you for being ignorant." The foot laughed and said, "When I am dirty, isn't it your 'hand' that washes my feet? When you want to pick something up, if I refuse to move, can you pick it up?" The hand was questioned by the foot and was rendered speechless. The foot continued, "In the world, no matter what happens, there is no noble or lowly distinction. Each has its own use. We must help each other to be effective."

Animal Feet 238

— Chi Fo

Little friends! It is very interesting to study various animals, big and small. Just looking at their 'feet', there are already all kinds of shapes and colors, which is very interesting.

Land animals all have feet. Some aquatic animals have feet that have turned into fins, and some have webbed feet. Why is this? Because land animals need feet to walk, and aquatic animals need fins or webs to swim. It's all because of adapting to the environment.

The feet of ferocious beasts have claws, which are convenient for tearing and eating other animals. The soles of their feet have thick flesh, so they make no noise when they walk, and they don't get hurt when they jump. The feet of carnivores such as tigers, leopards, cats, and lions are all like this. Clumsy beasts have hooves on their feet, some with double hooves and some with single hooves. Therefore, hoofed animals are divided into even-toed and odd-toed, such as elephants, cattle, sheep, etc., which are hoofed animals.

Birds are flying animals, with feet and claws. Insects all have six feet. Ducks are good at swimming, with webs growing in their feet, as are frogs. It's like a boat with oars. Fish's abdominal fins and pectoral fins are like oars, and the tail fin is like a rudder, which is really interesting.

Snakes, roundworms, pinworms, and hookworms have no feet, and they move entirely by the wriggling of their bodies. Frogs and deer have long hind legs and short forelegs, so they jump very fast. Crabs have eight feet, and giraffes, perhaps the 'kylin' mentioned by the ancients, have overly tall necks and all walk sideways. The front two feet of birds have turned into wings, so they can fly.

— Zhang Yuming

Cuckoo! Cuckoo!

You crow in the air.
