You deserve to be a beneficial bird!

Stevenson's Childhood 240

— Lin Ruan

Little friends, do you know the great British inventor Stevenson? The trains you see were invented by him. He was the son of a stoker at a coal mining company. When he was little, he only herded sheep for others. When he was fourteen, he started helping his father with work. But at the same time, he secretly studied. Later, his father died, and the whole family's clothes, poor things, depended on him alone. At that time, he also lost his wife, and his sadness was indescribable.

But Stevenson, who was not afraid of difficulties, started studying science regardless of whether he had the ability or not. The first time, he invented the safety lamp in the coal mine. The second time, he invented the railway, a powerful means of transportation. It was announced and performed on the road from Liverpool to Manchester, and the people watching cheered and wished him success, but in 1848, he died.

Little friends, a person who struggles, even if the environment is not good, cannot be stopped.

A Letter to Little City Friends 241

— Xu Zongjie

Dear Little Friends:

Your innocence, liveliness, and happiness are so enviable that I gave up the qualifications of a little old man - I am almost forty years old - and hang out with the children all day long, being the oldest old brother.

Little friends! I now live in the countryside, and can also be called an old brother from the countryside. What are some of the scenes and colors in the countryside in early summer? What do we play? Let me report some to you.

The rice seedlings in the field are already two inches long, planted in rows. The rapeseed has formed seeds, and the peas have also formed fruits. A kind of small bird is calling, "Quickly cuckoo! Quickly cuckoo!" The strong young men in the neighborhood have begun to take off their shoes, roll up their sleeves, and go to work in the fields.

The little friends and I get up together at five o'clock in the morning, walking and jumping on the bank of the field. There is a little wet dew in the grass, and the sun in the east has also begun to show its crimson face. We look at the rice seedlings in the field, look at the tadpoles in the stream, and listen to the birds singing on the branches. After walking like this for an hour, we each go home for breakfast, to school, and to do work.

Dusk is our happiest time. A large, soft, green lawn is our playground and natural chair. Many children are kicking balls, racing, or high jumping on it. We pick many wildflowers and weave them into crowns for the winners to wear. When we are tired of playing, we lie on it, tell stories, sing mountain songs, until the sun sets in the west, and Mr. Toad, who shouts slogans, cackles and calls for the meeting to end, and we each go back.

Little friends! How do you feel about these simple reports? Are you willing to try this rural life? I warmly welcome you to join us and wish you happiness. Your old brother, Xu Zongjie, sends his regards.

What is the Earth Like? 242

— Han Yu

Little friends! Do you know what the earth is like?

The shape of the earth is a sphere. To be more precise, its shape is like an orange. Little friends, if you don’t believe the earth is round, you can go to the seaside and look far at a ship coming from the front. We first see the ship's smokestack, and only later can we see the hull. If you think the earth is flat, we should see the hull and smokestack together. How can this phenomenon occur?

During a lunar eclipse, we can see a round shadow on the moon. This shadow is the shadow of the earth reflected onto the moon. The dark shadow is round, so of course the earth is also round.

Little friends may ask, if the earth is round and constantly moving, why don't we feel it at all? You can also catch an ant on a ball and spin the ball quickly, but the ant can still walk forward without feeling anything. This is because the ball is too big and the ant is too small. We are like many ants, but the earth is a very large ball.

About Grabbing Thirty 243

— Sheng Huai

Little friends! Last time, this publication published a small game called "Grabbing Thirty." I think you've already played it. I want to ask you, after playing, what experience did you gain?

Little friends! I am now writing down the experiences of "Grabbing Thirty" here. Do you want to know?

Step 1: Within ten numbers, grab three, six, and nine.

Step 2: From ten to twenty, grab two, five, and eight.

Step 3: From twenty to thirty, grab one, four, and seven.

If you grab in this way, you are guaranteed to get thirty. If you don't believe it, try it!

Sending Eggs 丨Sensory Game丨 244

— Yin

Whether a child's sensory perception is sensitive or not is indeed somewhat related to their innate physiology, but postnatal behavioral training is also very important. Even if a child is naturally dull and slow to perceive, if they are given very appropriate training, although they may not catch up to a gifted child, they can at least surpass children who have not received sensory training. The best training method is through games. This "Sending Eggs" game is one of the methods for training children's sensory sensitivity.

There is no limit to the number of people playing the game, but too few may reduce interest, and too many may make it difficult for the guesser, so five to ten people is the most suitable. The location of the game is also not limited; it can be indoors or outdoors. Before starting, first choose one person to be the "egg sender" and one person to be the "guesser." The remaining people put their hands behind their backs and stand against the wall. The guesser closes their eyes tightly and stands about ten steps away from the people standing against the wall. The egg sender prepares a small ball or stone to represent the egg. They can sing, "Mommy hen is sending eggs, who wants one? Who wants one?" While giving the egg to any child, they then say, "Sent it! Guess who got it, and I'll give it to you to eat!" The guesser then walks closer to the children standing against the wall, observes their faces, and guesses who received the egg. If they guess correctly, the receiver and the guesser switch roles. If they don't guess correctly, they guess again. If they don't guess correctly after three tries, they will be punished by singing a song or telling a story. The egg sender can swap the egg or give it away before handing it to someone. The children who received or didn't receive the egg can deliberately make strange expressions to make it difficult for the guesser to observe.

Magpies and Crows 245

— Da Qi

Magpies chirping bring good news, crows cawing foretell misfortune. This is a superstition. Magpies and crows are just birds; how can they know people's good or bad luck? However, some people know it's not to be relied upon, but when they hear a magpie chirping, they can't help but feel happy; when they hear a crow cawing, they can't help but feel disgusted. In fact, crows know to feed their parents, they are filial birds, not something terribly bad. People always curse them whenever they open their mouths. It's really unfair to them! However, the crow's caw is "wah, wah, wah," carrying a kind of sad sound, causing unpleasant feelings, making people somewhat unwilling to listen. If that crow is ignorant and nods its head at people, constantly cawing "wah, wah, wah," people will pick up stones and throw them to drive it away. Isn't this what we often see? Although magpies chirping aren't particularly good, they are comparatively more energetic and pleasing to the ear, so a few chirps don't matter, many chirps don't hurt, and they are always welcomed everywhere.

Little friends, from this, we can see that people's speech must also be proper. Writing has grammar, calligraphy has methods, painting has techniques. How can speaking not have methods? In ancient elementary schools, there was "etiquette of responding," which was the study of speaking. In the sage's school, there was "the subject of language," which also emphasized speaking. If speaking is improper, no matter how good your knowledge and character are, you will often invite resentment and jealousy whenever you speak, constantly bumping into walls, just like a crow, opening your mouth and causing people to despise you. How can you gain a foothold in society?

How to Draw a Black Cat 248

— Wu Song Bao

Umbrellas of the Past Three Thousand Years - Various Umbrellas Past and Present 249

— He Gongchao

(1) Umbrellas of the Ancient Egyptians (2) Umbrellas on Assyrian Two-Wheeled Chariots (3) Umbrellas of Assyrian Nobles (4) Umbrellas of the Greeks (5) Umbrellas of the Romans (6) Ancient Chinese Umbrellas (7) Umbrellas of Siamese Nobles (8) Umbrellas of the Japanese (9) Umbrellas of the Ashanti People (10) Sandals in the Sandal Dance (11) Modern Umbrellas

Umbrellas have existed since ancient times. They were a symbol of authority used by kings and nobles. In ancient Egyptian and Assyrian carvings, we can see a servant holding an umbrella behind a king or noble, indicating that he was a person of authority. Umbrellas spread from the above two places to Greece and Rome, but became tools for shielding from sunlight. However, in Eastern countries, umbrellas are still considered symbols of authority, such as in Siam, Malaya, and places like Ashanti and Abyssinia in Africa. In ancient China, umbrellas also had a solemn and noble meaning. But in modern times, they are only used as tools for avoiding rain and shielding from the sun, or as decorations for women, as in Japan and China.

Women's Garden

On Nurseries and Public Childcare 250

— Zi Jiu

Since the news of the establishment of "nurseries" in Shanghai, it has attracted general attention. In the supplement of this newspaper on May 13th, there was an article by Mr. Shi Shi, "On Nurseries and Public Childcare." It was against nurseries, generally saying: "Although the public childcare of children in European and American countries has been implemented and has achieved results, considering the current social situation, national economy, cultural level, and family concepts in our country, it is considered that there are still doubts about promoting public childcare for children." The reasons for opposing are roughly no more than two points: (1) Opposing women engaging in professions and neglecting childcare. (2) Doubts about the nature of public childcare for children itself.

Regarding the first point, Mr. Shi Shi said: "The pursuit of professions by general women in China today is actually just selling short-term youth... After marriage, since society cannot retain suitable positions for mothers with children, then nurseries naturally lose the necessity of existence. Moreover, women have the natural duty of raising children. Raising children to make them physically and mentally healthy is serving society, and its value is better than being a vase in an organization or a living signboard in a commercial arena." The need for women to engage in professions, even if leaving aside doctrines and theories, only speaking of the current situation in China, due to years of imperialist aggression, the prevalence of internal strife, rural bankruptcy, and the recession of the market, middle-class and lower-class housewives have had no choice but to seek employment to make ends meet. As for women from upper-middle-class families, since they have already had the opportunity to receive education, and have knowledge and skills, naturally they also want to develop their instincts, engage in politics, academics, or other professions, to the best of their abilities. Therefore, women's pursuit of professions is an inevitable phenomenon in today's society. On the one hand, there are working women, and on the other hand, there is a need for childcare institutions. One side can concentrate on work, and the other side can provide mass education. Those who like to work, work; those who like to raise children, raise children. It can be said that there is a division of labor for individuals and cooperation for society. As for the so-called pursuing professions, which is merely selling short-term youth, it is truly a defamatory remark against working women. But we cannot deny that there are indeed many working women who give up their professions after marriage, or cannot continue to engage in professions. The former is a phenomenon of a society where there is too little porridge for too many monks, and the reasons for the latter are certainly varied, but it is also due to the lack of childcare institutions.

Regarding the second point, Mr. Shi Shi believes that public childcare for children will destroy family relationships, so he says, "Children and families have an inseparable relationship. Children are the center of family happiness... Only children and grandchildren around the knees can constitute family harmony... Family is also a paradise for children. Parental love is the only food for children's lives, otherwise, it will be difficult to survive." Mr. Shi Shi is still yearning for that kind of feudalistic peaceful paradise of having children and grandchildren around the knees. In fact, in today's society, where affairs are increasingly complex and making a living is not easy, it is already impossible for middle-class and lower-class families to enjoy this leisurely family life. Moreover, nurseries are different from China's inherent infant asylums. The children raised in nurseries must still return home on time to reunite with their parents. As for whether the family is a paradise for children, it is actually questionable, and the facts tell us that Chinese families, in general, are hells for children. The rich do not know how to teach, do not know how to raise, only know how to spoil; the poor cannot even talk about raising. Moreover, Chinese children, because they are accustomed to family life and lack group cultivation, generally have a sand-like habit, which is half formed by family life. As for parental love, it is indeed spiritual food for children, but doting and selfish love || parents regard children as playthings, as private property || loving them is actually harming them, not only harming the children themselves, but also causing harm to society. The high mortality rate of Chinese children is unparalleled. There are certainly many reasons, but it is also due to not knowing how to teach, not knowing how to raise, and being caused by hunger and cold. In this situation, there is a need for public and more scientific methods of teaching and raising.

Regarding the issue of fees, according to the general practice in advanced countries, it is mostly based on the income of the parents of young children and has nothing to do with the number of children.

Mr. Shi Shi concluded by saying: "In fact, it only opens the door for licentious playboys, and the result may become the origin of illegitimate children and adulterous children." In recent years, the rampant flow of human desires has been a well-known fact. Then the proliferation of illegitimate children and adulterous children may be an inevitable phenomenon. This bad phenomenon is a social disease. Illegitimate children or adulterous children are inherently innocent. Moreover, the Chinese nation was formerly 400 million, and now it may be less than that number. For the sake of revitalizing the nation, I believe that regardless of whether they are illegitimate children or legitimate children, it is necessary to find ways to make them grow up healthy. Therefore, I am glad that Shanghai will soon have nurseries appearing, and I hope that more and more will be established in cities and towns. However, I hope that those who run nurseries will strive for scientific management, avoid being aristocratic, and, even more, hope to open the door to convenience for poor children.

Opinions of Great World Thinkers on Women's Issues (8) 251

— Hua

VII. Robert Owen

Robert Owen was a great Utopian thinker from England, born in 1771 and died in 1858. During this time, the progress of technology in British production had turned a large number of skilled artisans into appendages of machines, or completely excluded them from production and replaced them with unskilled, weak women and children. This was the period of capitalism's "rampant evils." Whole batches of young children died due to being cruelly exploited in factories. Owen was born in this era and witnessed all kinds of tragedies, which turned him from a great industrialist and humanitarian into a thorough social reformer.

The scope of his social reforms was very broad, including protecting children, running education, establishing schools, establishing nurseries, protecting factory labor, opening hospitals, and providing relief to the elderly and the unemployed. In order to realize his ideals, Owen attempted to establish a kind of communist commune to replace the old, dying system. But he did not understand that the economic emancipation of labor and liberation from slavery must be the responsibility of labor itself. Owen believed that "wise and far-sighted people" from all parties could jointly realize the necessary reforms.

When Owen was ten years old, his father sent him to work as an apprentice in a shop in the countryside. Later, he worked for several years in the two major cities of London and Manchester. In 1790, Owen, at the age of nineteen, became the manager of a large yarn factory in Manchester (which was then the center of the British textile industry). Seven years later, he and his friends jointly bought a yarn factory in New Lanark, Scotland, for 1.25 million marks, with 3,000 male and female workers and children. This factory became his laboratory for social reform plans.

Owen's first task was to pay attention to children. He set up many nurseries to accommodate children over six months old, in order to alleviate the suffering of female workers with children. He abolished the methods of rewarding and punishing children in the schools he ran; his factories also did not employ children under the age of ten; those over ten years old were required to work for twelve and a half hours, which was a huge step forward at the time, because even a four-year-old child had to work for twelve to sixteen hours in a factory at that time.

In 1825, in order to realize his ideal of a new social system, Owen purchased a piece of land in Indiana, USA, and established a communist community called "New Harmony." Owen had many outstanding male and female comrades-in-arms here, among whom a Ms. Blight played a particularly important role in the women's movement. She personally established a small group within "New Harmony." After the failure of the experiment at "New Harmony," Ms. Blight continued to fight for many years to win equal rights for women.

Owen believed that women were born equal to men and had no obligation to obey men. He also bravely put his beliefs into practice in life, although this caused violent attacks on him by society, he remained unyielding. In "New Harmony," women enjoyed the right to vote and be elected. In the "Young America" magazine run by his son, he published his twelve demands, one of which was "men and women should be completely equal."

Owen deeply believed in the power of the highest ideals of mankind. He attempted to create an example of a new, more perfect, collective social life system to counter the brutal exploitation of the time. In every aspect, he revealed a wealth of thought, which was the object of ridicule and sarcasm at the time, and now it has become the treasure of international socialism.

As for Owen's opinions on marriage, prostitution, women's occupations, and children's education, I will discuss them next time.

Alluring Mannerisms and Women's Liberation 252

— Jiong

Recently, a movement of alluring mannerisms for women is being promoted in Cleveland, USA.

It is said that the rise of this movement of alluring mannerisms is based on pleasing men. Because men feel that women who wear makeup are simply vases, soulless and only for people to admire. This not only fails to produce lively postures, but also has adverse effects on health. How can it "please the noble?" Therefore, they, standing from the perspective of pleasing men, found: (1) Because the number of women with lung disease is increasing day by day, it is not easy to cure disease and prolong life without promoting the movement of alluring mannerisms. (2) Displaying alluring mannerisms is also an opportunity for women to exercise their bodies, making them healthier day by day, and making it impossible for illnesses to invade. (3) It is not considered beauty for women to decorate their faces with cosmetics. It is only with charming postures that they are fully beautiful. (4) One must work hard on alluring mannerisms to be pursued by men everywhere. For these reasons, the movement of alluring mannerisms was launched: lectures are held everywhere, slogans are posted, and even various women's organizations have established specialized schools for the study of alluring mannerisms, teaching how to be alluring to men, how to be alluring to lovers, how to be alluring to husbands, as well as the alluring mannerisms of narration, love, greetings, farewells, and walking, so that they become experts in pleasing men before stopping. Can it be said that this can contribute to the women's liberation movement?

We know that the reason why women are in a position of oppression is due to social systems and economic conditions. This can be understood by simply flipping through the history of social evolution and the history of the women's liberation movement. And the American women, after being addicted to the taste of makeup, are coming up with a new trick: they mistakenly believe that by working hard on alluring mannerisms and being pursued by men everywhere, showing their health and arrogance, they are liberated (?). This is simply a self-deceiving joke!

If we believe that things from the West are always "modern" and learn this alluring mannerism, then our 200 million women under double oppression will be disarming themselves and abolishing the battlefront for demanding liberation. Because this kind of alluring mannerism movement presents us with a posture of pleasing men. It is a huge rock blocking the future of the women's liberation movement. It is a cup of anesthetic soup. Therefore, we should resolutely prevent the intrusion of this alluring mannerism movement and strengthen our women's movement front, strive hard from the economic and political aspects, and then we can obtain true liberation!

Do You Believe It? Twins Can Actually Have Two Fathers 253

— Wu

Not long ago, a strange case of twins being able to have two fathers, which shocked society, occurred in South Dakota, USA, and the local court also set a new precedent that had never existed in the world for this matter. Readers, do you believe it? This is really true, because in the village of Pullman in that state, there was a farmer named Yadva Bard, who had two identical twins, one of whom had a face very similar to Bard, while the other one was not like Bard at all. Therefore, Bard was very suspicious. Also, because his wife had committed adultery with someone else, Bard obtained evidence, and thus the dispute began. Bard said: He can only fulfill his father's obligation to his own child (that is, the one with the similar face), as for the other one, it is definitely not his child and can only be the responsibility of the mother. As a result, the couple took it to the state court. Naturally, Bard's reasons were very sufficient. After several interrogations by the court, Judge Dully Berger finally ruled to grant Bard's request, with the husband and wife sharing the support of the two children. According to this, twins can really have two fathers, can't they?

Echoes of "A Woman's Heart" 254

— Jue

"You are wrong!"

Sir:

In the tenth issue of Women's Garden, your sad history was published. At the end, you said, "Who is willing to say to me, 'You are right,' or 'You are wrong'?" According to my use of all my superficial knowledge to "criticize" (?), I dare to say with certainty: "You are wrong!"

Please don't doubt that I am speaking against my conscience. In defending my gender.

First: I feel that when you were just starting to love each other, you certainly had to use all your abilities to observe your object. Aren't newspapers and magazines now full of news of marital deception? Can you suddenly believe that your object will not be the protagonist in those news stories? Looking closely at your "A Woman's Heart," you don't seem to have noticed this point at all.

Second: Since you knew that not long before you fell in love, he had been passionately in love with another woman, you should have inquired into why he broke up with his first lover and how he broke up with his first lover. Of course, he would use deceptive and improper means to break away from you, and his means of breaking away from his first lover must also be none other than deception or other improper methods. But according to you, you knew that "it is said that she refused to agree to his request, and then they broke up."

He would break up with his first lover because she did not agree to his certain request. Can you guarantee that he would not break up with you because you did not agree to his request to love another woman?

Third: Since your good friend warned you, "Can you believe that he will not go on to passionately love a third woman?" Why did you suddenly believe him? He would smash the precious lute given to him by his teacher, which means that he is a fellow who is good at forgetting friends. People who write blood letters are often the people with the weakest will. People who use death to threaten are also the worst dregs of humanity. You cannot be moved by his blood letter; you cannot abandon your doubts and hesitation for his "death." Death! Don't you know that many compatriots in the Northeast were brutally killed by the violent Japanese? Don't you know that many compatriots in the Northwest were drowned and starved to death by natural disasters? Don't you know that many commoners with round heads and square feet were shot to death by warlords? What is so great about the death of a person who would smash the precious lute given to him by his teacher in order to deceive the love of a member of the opposite sex!

Also, fourth: You cannot hate why your heart is not "ruthless" and not "poisonous." Your failure is not due to your heart being not "ruthless" and not "poisonous," but due to your brain lacking rationality! Your heart is too easily moved.

With these four points, I dare say that you are wrong. But, sir, you are from Hunan. People from Hunan and people from Guangdong are both the most courageous people in our country, the most enterprising people, the most revolutionary people, and the most hopeful people. I respectfully wish you to be able to use the blood of us Hunan people to break through the vastness of your future!

Letters to the Editor 257

(1) Sir, Upon reviewing your newspaper's "Women's Enclosure" column on May 13, an article titled "Our School" mentioned that the school forbids reading "Cuore" and conducts virginity examinations, and generally referred to the authorities' oppression of students. At the end, there was an editor's note stating that this article was submitted by a student from Qingdao Municipal Girls' Middle School, and the author claimed responsibility, but questioned whether the content was fabricated. Please be aware of those in charge of education administration in the local area. Your newspaper's concern for girls' education is appreciated, but this article is not a faithful record. The language attacking the school authorities is very obvious, and the sections referring to the prohibition of reading "Cuore" and the virginity examination are especially untrue. We would like to inform your newspaper editor of the facts verified by our bureau. The school pays great attention to the physical and mental education of students. Therefore, the school stipulates that teachers and staff should regularly review students' extracurricular reading materials. Any books that are not suitable for the cultivation of young people's physical and mental health are advised not to be read by students. As for the book "Cuore," the school's library has always displayed it. How can there be a prohibition on reading it? Regarding physical examinations, as the editor said, the school regards it as a method of promoting students' health, so there are two types of examinations: disease examination and physical examination. The former is purely for examining diseases and is conducted by the school doctor, while the latter is mostly for examining the development of the body and is conducted by physical education teachers and staff from the Department of Student Affairs. This physical examination was conducted by three female teachers to examine whether the students' bodies had normal development and whether their clothing hindered hygiene, and there was absolutely no virginity examination. More than 300 students underwent the examination without any coercion. What the article said was exploiting the topic and sensationalizing, and it was not likely to have been written by a student of the school. However, since the submission claimed to take responsibility for the article, please (omission) grant a factual correction to clarify the truth and we look forward to your reply. The Qingdao Education Bureau, May 18, to the Shanghai Shenbao.

(2) Sir: I have just read the article "My School" in your newspaper's Women's Garden on May 13. It contains many insulting and slanderous words against our school, and it is said that it was submitted by a student of our school, which is very shocking. According to the rules, disease examinations are conducted every semester in our school. This semester, on March 5 (Health Week), in addition to inviting Dr. Jiao, the school doctor, to give a lecture on "Health Issues" during Memorial Week, disease examinations began in the afternoon after class. The school doctor was responsible for the examinations, and nurses from the Municipal Hospital and staff from the Department of Student Affairs assisted. The examinations were conducted on the ears, eyes, teeth, throat, and heart and lungs to see if there were any diseases, and the results were entered into the disease examination form item by item. The intention was to implement effective treatment or prevention based on the examination results to improve the students' health. On March 7, physical examinations were also conducted, and female physical education teachers were responsible. Staff from the Department of Student Affairs and female English teachers assisted in everything. The examinations were conducted on the posture of the head, shoulders, back, spine, abdomen, and feet, as well as the strength of the grip, and the results were entered into the physical examination form so that appropriate corrections could be made to obtain the correct posture. This work was completed within three weeks. As for the "virginity examination," not only had Mr. "never heard of it before,"

our school had never even thought about it, let alone implemented it! As for the sections prohibiting reading "Cuore," they are unfounded and ridiculous, and there is no need to explain them. Rumors stop with the wise. The so-called "although the content is questionable, the author claims responsibility, so let's disclose it" and "the aforementioned situation, if not fabricated" show that Mr. also suspects and speaks cautiously! However, rumors confuse the public and affect the reputation of the school, so our school cannot remain silent. We have specially described the facts and ask your publication to disclose a correction, (omission) To Mr. Han of the Women's Garden of the Shenbao, Qingdao Municipal Girls' Middle School, May 18.

Note: The editor of this publication is not surnamed Han. The so-called Mr. Han is unknown.

US New Cotton Growing Well 271

New York, 25th: A report on the cotton market for the past week states that the development of the silver situation last week has disappointed inflationists. The cotton market loosened due to our long position liquidation, scattered selling, and good progress in new cotton growth. At the same time, the cotton goods market is sluggish, and the value of gold dollars is stable. However, it later rebounded slightly due to short covering. There is a lack of pressure from the South, but transaction volume has also decreased, so market fluctuations are very narrow. Sprouting of new cotton in the eastern part is slightly poor, but other areas are generally progressing well. It is now known that 90% to 95% of the new cotton has been planted, but opinions on the cotton fields cannot be realized until the end of June. It is necessary to wait for a complete decision on the planters' opposition to the Peng Hai Plan's allocation. Currently, market prices are fluctuating between strong spot positions, good new cotton growth, and poor cotton goods conditions.

Wheat Prices Unlikely to Rise Before New Grain Arrival 273

Yesterday, the future wheat market was generally flat. Although quoted prices for foreign wheat were high, rising by 90 cents to $1, the market no longer seemed to pay attention to foreign wheat prices. This is because, according to reports from various locations in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, the domestic new wheat crop is very abundant. Even in Henan and Shaanxi provinces, the current situation indicates a good harvest. Furthermore, foreign wheat and old wheat are sufficient until the new crop arrives. Even in the one or two months after the new crop arrives, there will be little need for wholesale purchases. With the market understanding this, price increases are unlikely. As a result, prices for July and August were unchanged, and prices for September were slightly lower by 1 cent. Spot wheat demand was low as factories had access to foreign wheat, so no transactions were reported.

Flour Market Remains Sluggish 274

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market, prices for all months showed a flat and sluggish trend. Quoted prices for foreign wheat rose by around 90 cents to $1 in Chicago, and by 90 cents in Canada. At the opening, the market was relatively stable due to high prices for foreign wheat. However, customer demand remained lackluster. Although the new wheat crop will arrive soon, the fear of oversupply persisted, and there was no urgent buying interest. Therefore, despite the rise in foreign wheat prices, it did not seem to have much impact, and the market remained sluggish. Transactions were even quieter in the afternoon session. Although small and medium-sized factories wanted to offer their inventory, few buyers were interested. After some haggling, prices stabilized slightly. As a result, prices for the current month were better by 5 li, prices for June, July, and August were better by 2.5 li, prices for September were better by 7.5 li, and prices for October were better by 5 li.

Silk and Tea - Zhejiang Silkworm Cocoon Harvest Is Abundant, Jiangsu Silkworms Lack Leaves 279

▲ In Hangzhou County, many local silkworms were hatched early this year in the villages surrounding the city. When the weather was cold and rainy at first, 60%-70% of the worms died. For this reason, late silkworms were raised to make up for it and the improved breed hatched later, but with good care, there were hardly any losses. After their long sleep, the weather was sunny and warm and the silkworms developed well. Early silkworm cocoons have already gone on the market and cocoon trading firms such as Jinglun have opened one after the other. Arrivals on the market are not abundant and there are more local silkworm cocoons which are lower quality. At first, cocoons were priced at $18 and the improved breed was at $20. The silkworm farmers were not happy to sell so cheap so the price all rose $4-5.

▲ Around Pingyao in places such as Jinjialong Village, there was not enough economic activity this year so many local silkworms were hatched. The weather wasn’t right and the worms’ resistance was poor and they were heavily damaged. Afterwards, improved breeds were raised and with effort, the results were okay. New cocoons are already on the market and the cocoons are on average just 50%-60% full. The improved silkworm breed’s cocoons are higher quality. Silkworm cocoons of the local breed are just $20-$24 whereas improved silkworm cocoons are $32-$33. The market is looking bullish.

▲ In the Chang’an improved silkworm area, most of the farmers raised improved breeds of silkworms. Even if the weather was cold, the influence was minor. The silkworms were late and developed best during their long sleep. Early and late silkworm cocoons successively entered the market and the cocoon trading firms have been open for four days. The receipt quantity is low. Silkworm cocoons of the local breed are $25-$26 whereas improved breed cocoons are $35. The silkworm farmers all must take a loss.

▲ Most farmers in the cities and villages surrounding Danyang raised the local breed of silkworms due to economic concerns. Because spring was cold and rainy, there was a lot of damage. Many of the silkworms had leaves dumped out and were replaced with improved breeds. After their second sleep, the weather was sunny and warm and the worms developed very well. The early ones had a vigorous long sleep and the late ones had just begun to sleep. Occasionally there would be those who were having their third sleep and beginning to leaf. Many mulberry trees in the surrounding villages have been dug up for firewood in recent years leading to a shortage of feed for the silkworms and there wasn’t enough supply to meet demand. Leaf prices had risen to over $2.

Wuyuan Tea Output Has an Acidic Harvest 282

Wuyuan Green Tea, the mountain farmer is already at the opening garden picking stage and has been manufacturing for one week. Appropriately, the weather has been good during this week. Dew falls in the mornings. The tea buds had been green and weak due to excess rain but after sun and dew, their taste deepened. The taste of the manufactured dried tea, the aroma, and the color were excellent, something unseen in recent years. The tea firms were delighted by this beautiful weather. As of today (the 17th), the tea leaves in the various villages had been picked and manufactured for the most part. The gardens are ready to be shut down in one week. But the tea from the shady side of the mountains and the tea from the plains was stunted because it had been frozen in the snow last winter and the mountain farmers reported bad harvests across the board. The overall total of tea produced across the county is estimated to be 30% lower than last year. The mountain farmers had been stuck with bad economics and bankruptcy for a long time and had been hoping for a good tea harvest to slightly increase their income. Now that it's like this, they can’t help but be depressed and disappointed. It is raining heavily today and the mountain farmers have stopped picking. Because the tea will soon have been picked, the firm is ready to go out to the farms to explore the prices. Looking at the state of things, it seems the mountain prices offered will be around $50.

Yixian Tea Output Has an Acidic Harvest 283

Yixian is a district of Anhui known for tea with the most output. In places such as the eleven-and-a-half Capital, Yuanyuan, Zikeng, Kaoxi, Lucun, and Dongyuan, it’s been tea picking season for over a week, but because the climate in places such as Liyuan and Yuanyuan has been too cold, the tea buds have merely come out as green buds and have been hard to pick. With the weather warming in recent days and new tea from everywhere on the market, each mountain farmer is getting ready to open their gardens. According to the mountain farmers, the tea trees in each village were damaged by snow last winter and are growing poorly. The amount of output in the future will be estimated to be 70% of what it was in the past. But the tender shoots and quality of the tea produced are better than in the past. At the moment, in addition to the existing tea firms, Ggongxing and Tongyang have newly opened on Jicun Street and are preparing to do business. The market trend is booming.

Shaoxing Tea Industry Is Not Thriving 284

Pingshui YaoGuo town in Shaoxing is close to mountain villages and is an important tea-producing area for Zhejiang province. The quantity exported is no less than Suichun. In 1918-1919, the mountain farmers there saw how the sales of disc tea were sluggish and business was difficult and were determined to remake the tea into banner tea to find a new way out. Whenever new tea entered the market, the tea merchants of Suzhou, Hangzhou, Shanghai, and Guangzhou would all carry money to the production area to search for purchases. For over 10 years, business has been prosperous. But in recent years due to the influence of banditry and all kinds of taxes and fees levied again and again, buyers everywhere have not come one after another. And so business has not been thriving and has nearly fallen off a cliff. At the moment, tea firms in the area that purchase for customers have also lost money, and it’s hard to support them with the money they have left. Just one or two tea firms in the town are preparing to open this year. At the moment, it’s quiet and the scene is desolate.

Yushan Tea Market Revives 285

Yushan Green Tea in Jiangxi province had long relied on foreign firms as its greatest ally. Later, because of poor manufacturing methods, sales slowed as a result. Businessmen were ruined and customers stopped coming due to years of banditry. It was nearly as if there was no tea market to speak of for the past 5 years. Last year, just one firm in the county set up business and the decline had reached an extreme. Recently, the Red bandits in the county have been surrounded and wiped out by national armies and have gradually been pacified. Tea merchants in Chengcun Street, Xiaoyushan, and elsewhere saw that Shanghai valued cheap good and that the mountain price in the producing area was average. The good could be exported by means of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railroad and transportation was convenient. They all devised ways to restore their old business. In total, there are 9 tea firms opening business this year and it is estimated that another three or four firms are brewing preparations. The market scene is one of revival.

Qimen Black Tea Market Prices Trending Down 286

Since Qimen Black Tea started opening scales and purchasing last month, the first good that was purchased was poor quality because the weather had been unceasingly rainy. The firm sought to protect its assets and bought in. Furthermore, production fell sharply and each firm’s purchasing quantity was extremely small. The most amount of head good that was made a pile was only a hundred crates and less than that was just fifty or sixty crates. The small crate amount was the least seen in decades. Even if the weather has become better this month and production has been more vigorous, the tea trees are growing unevenly and the tea could be done within days. Market prices have also not been constantly trending up and down. Every 100 catties started at an offered price of $48 which successively rose to $84 and $100. This week, it fell sharply to just over $30. Market prices are trending down every day. Every firm’s head crate of good has finally been piled up, opened, and is being transported. But the bandits in Daohu are still strong, Qifu crate of tea must be transported to Shanghai roundaboutly by Tunxi and Hangzhou.
